\num{2} \eng{dog wags tail} nAyi (saMtoVSa sUcisalu) bAla alAlxDisutatxde. 
\num{3} \eng{the tail wags the dog} samAjada, yA pakaSxda kaniSaThx vayxkitx samAjavanenxV, pakaSxvanenxV, ADisutAtxne, naDesutitxdAdxne, alAlxDisutitxdAdxne; bAla nAyiyanenxV alAlxDisutitxde yA bAlada pArupatayxvAgi hoVgide.

\bentry

\pron{veVjf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\banum
\alnum{a} (kAmiRkana \vi) (dina)kUli; kaMbaLa. 
\alnum{b} (nwkarana \vi) saMbaLa: \eng{he gets good wages} avanige oLeLxya veVtana doreyutatxde. \eng{at a wage of Rs.40 a week} vArakokxmemx \eng{40} rU. meVrege. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\rUpa) (\Eva\ yA \bava dalilx) parxtiPala: \eng{the wages of sin is death} pApakekx parxtiPala maqtuyxveV, maraNaveV. 
\num{3} (\athaRshA) (\bava dalilx) kAmiRka veVtana; oTuTx utApxdaneyalilx baMDavALagArarige salulxva parxtiPalavanunx biTuTx, kAmiRkarige parxtiPala niVDuva saluvAgiyeV parxteyxVkisi miVsaliTaTx BAga.

\bentry
\word[wait(1)]{wait} 
\pron{veVTf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} samaya kAyutitxru; sariyAda avakAshakAkxgi kAyutitxru: \eng{he is waiting his opportunity} avanu sariyAda avakAshakAkxgi, samayakAkxgi kAyutitxdAdxne. \eng{you must wait your turn} niVnu ninanx saradigAgi kAyutitxrabeVku. \eng{wait my convenience} nanage anukUlavAguvavaregU kAdiru, tALu. 
\num{2} (UTa \mo vugaLigAgi beVrobabxra Agamanavanunx niriVkiSxsutAtx) kAdiru. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (kAyaR, parxyANa, \mo vugaLa \vi) (hesarisida kAlada yA niriVkiSxsida GaTaneyavaregU) taDe; tALu; kAyu; kAdiru: \eng{wait a minute} oMdu nimiSa tALu. \eng{he waited (for) an hour} avanu oMdu GaMTe hotutx kAdidadx. \eng{I shall not wait any longer} nAnu inunx muMde kAyuvudilalx. \eng{he kept me waiting} (\engit{or} \eng{he made me wait)} avanu nananxnunx kAyuvaMte mADida. \eng{I have a month to wait yet} nAnu inUnx oMdu tiMgaLa kAla kAdirabeVkAgide. \eng{I will do it for you while you wait} niVnu kAyutitxruvaSaTxralilx nAnu ninagAgi adanunx mADutetxVne. 
\num{2} nidhAnisu; tALu; avasara paDabeVDa; taDe: \eng{wait till I come} nAnu baruvavaregU taDe, nidhAnisu. 
\num{3} eduru noVDu; niriVkiSxsu; kAyu: \eng{wait for high water} kaDala ubabxrakAkxgi kAyutitxru. \eng{he waited to see what would happen} EnAguvudoV noVDoVNaveMdu avanu kAdidadx. 
\num{4} rasetx \mo vugaLa pakakxdalilx savxlapxhotutx vAhanavanunx nililxsu, `pAkfR' mADu. 
\numi{5} 
\banum
\alnum{a} obabxra anukUla samayakAkxgi kAyu; veVLe kAyu. 
\alnum{b} OleYsu; seVvisu. 
\alnum{c} paricArike mADu; upacarisu. 
\alnum{d} (gwravAthaR) BeVTi niVDu; dashaRna mADu; saMdashiRsu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} (\pArxparx) obabxna anucaranAgi, beMgAvalAgi, mayARdegAgi -- joteyalilx hoVgu. 
\num{7} anusarisi, anugatavAgi, PalavAgi -- baru, odagu, saMBavisu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{he cannot wait} avanu kAyalAra; avanige tALemx ilalx. 
\num{2} \eng{that can wait} adanunx taDediDabahudu; adakekxVnU avasaravilalx; adanunx kUDaleV mADabeVkAgilalx. 
\num{3} \eng{wait and see} EneVnAgutatxdeyoV kAdu noVDutitxru. 
\num{4} \eng{wait at} [\engit{or}} (\ame) \eng{on] table} UTada meVjina baLi mANiyAgi yA paricArakanAgi vatiRsu, kAdiru. 
\numi{5} \eng{wait for it}! (\AmA) 
\banum
\alnum{a} adakAkxgi kAdiru! sariyAda kaSxNa baruvavaregU adanunx pArxraMBisabeVDa. 
\alnum{b} (aniriVkiSxtavAda yA soVjigada saMgatiyanunx heVLuvAga keVLugarige kAtaravanunxMTumADalu heVLuva) savxlapx -- tALi, taDeyiri, heVLutetxVne (eMba mAtu). 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{wait for me}! nanagAgi kAdiru! nananxnunx biTuTx hoVgibiDabeVDa. 
\num{7} \eng{wait on} (\AseTxrXV\ matutx nUyxsiZVleMDf matutx \kanu\ iMgalxMDf) tALemxyiMdiru; kAyu. 
\num{8} \eng{wait up} (obabxra Agamanavanunx niriVkiSxsutAtx) ececxtitxru; niderx mADade yA malagade kAdiru. 
\numi{9} \eng{wait (up)on} 
\banum
\alnum{a} obabxna anukUlakAkxgi kAdiru. 
\alnum{b} gaNayxvayxkitxge gwravasUcaka BeVTi niVDu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{10} \eng{you wait}! taDe, taDe! mADutetxVne! (shikiSxsutetxVneMba bedarike).

\emng

\pron{veVkf} 
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ \eng{woke} \ucAcx\ voVkf yA \eng{waked}; \BUkaq}
 \eng{woken} \ucAcx\ voVkanf yA \eng{waked}). 

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (niderxyiMda) ebibxsu; ecacxrisu; ecacxramADu; ecacxragoLisu; jAgaqtagoLisu (\rUpa\ saha): \eng{spring wakes all nature} vasaMtavu nisagaRvanenxlalx jAgaqtagoLisutatxde, ecacxragoLisutatxde. \eng{the shouting woke the echoes} A kUgu parxtidhavxnigaLanunx ebibxsitu. \eng{he woke up to the fact that he had been swindled} tAnu moVsakekx tutAtxgidedxVneMba satAyxMshakekx avanu ecacxragoMDa, satAyxMshavanunx avanu aritukoMDa. 
\numi{2} (jaDate, mAMdayx, \mo vugaLiMda) 
\banum
\alnum{a} ecacxragoLisu; jAgaqtagoLisu. 
\alnum{b} curukAgisu; caTuvaTikeyiMdiruvaMte mADu. 
\alnum{c} ariyuvaMte, gamanisuvaMte mADu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (satatxvananunx, satatxdadxnunx) punarujijxVvanagoLisu; ecacxragoLisu. 
\num{4} (gadadxladiMda, gadadxla ebibxsi) mwnavanunx, nishashxbadxteyanunx -- BaMgagoLisu; parxtidhavxni ebibxsu. 
\enum
\emng

\gl{\akirx}

\bentry
\word[walk(2)]{walk} 
\pron{vAkf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} naDage; naDageya riVti yA veVga; naDe: \eng{go at a walk} naDageya veVgadalilx hoVgu \eng{never gets beyond a walk} naDageya veVgakikxMta miVri naDeyalAra. \eng{I know him by his walk} avana naDageyiMda avananunx gurutisutetxVne. 
\num{2} naDageyalilx, naDageya veVgadalilx, (sathxLadiMda sathxLakekx) iruva dUra: \eng{it is only ten minutes' walk from here} adu ililxMda keVvala hatutx nimiSagaLa naDageya dUra(dalilxde). 
\num{3} pAdayAterx; kAlunaDageyalilx mADuva parxvAsa yA sutAtxTa, tirugATa; vAyxyAmakAkxgi mADuva aDADxTa, vihAra; gALisaMcAra: \eng{go for} (\engit{or} \eng{take) a walk} sutAtxTakekx hoVgu, gALi saMcArakekx (naDedu) hoVgu. 
\num{4} (dhamARthaRvAgi yA beVre kAraNakAkxgi vAgAdxna mADiruva haNavanunx gaLisalikAkxgi) pAdayAterx; kAlunaDageyalilx mADida parxyANa. 
\num{5} (vayxkitxge) pirxyavAda sutAtxTada mAgaR. 
\num{6} (tirugu vAyxpAri, aMceyavanu, \mo vara) sutAtxTada dAri. 
\num{7} pathikara ODATakAkxgiyeV mADiruva dAri; pAdacAri patha; kAludAri. 
\num{8} beVTenAyiya mariyanunx adara bagebageya parisarakekx ogigxsaloVsuga kaLuhisuva sathxLa. 
\num{9} koVLi paMdayxda huMjavanunx iDuva sathxLa. 
\num{10} kAvaligana BAga; obabx kAvalugArana kAvalige oLapaTaTx araNayxda BAga.

\bentry
\word[wall(1)]{wall} 
\pron{vAlf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} (kalulx, iTiTxge, kAMkirxVTf, marada dimimx yA halage, \mo vugaLiMda kaTiTxda, Uru, mane, koThaDi, gadedx, hola, toVTa, \mo vanunx parxteyxVkisuva) 
\banum
\alnum{a} goVDe; Bititx; kuDayx. 
\alnum{b} (AvaraNakAkxgi kaTiTxda) pwLi. 
\alnum{c} (deVvAlaya \mo vugaLa) pArxkAra. 
\alnum{d} (rakaSxNegAgi kaTiTxda) koVTe (goVDe). 
\alnum{e} aDaDxgoVDe; muMde sAgalu aDiDxyAguva -- goVDe, taDe, parxtibaMdhaka: \eng{we must break down the walls between community and community} jAtijAtigaLa naDuvaNa aDaDxgoVDegaLanunx, aDiDxgaLanunx, nAvu oDeduhAkabeVku. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (citarxgaLu \mo vanunx parxdashiRsuva koThaDi, \mo vugaLa) goVDe. 
\numi{3} (noVTakekx yA pariNAmadalilx) goVDeyaMtiruva vasutx; kuDayxpArxyavAdadudx: 
\banum
\alnum{a} pavaRtada kaDidAda pAshavxR. 
\alnum{b} rakaSxNe: \eng{a wall of steel bayonets} ukikxna saniVnugaLa kApugoVDe, rakaSxNA sAlu. 
\alnum{c} aDataDe: \eng{a wall of indifference} upeVkeSxya taDegoVDe, taDegaTuTx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} (oLage ToLALxgiruva yAvudeV vasutxvina yA racaneya) horameY; Bititx. 
\num{5} (\aMrashA, \pArxvi\ matutx \savi) aMga, jiVvANu, \mo vugaLa -- Bititx, koVsha, pore, horapadara. 
\num{6} (\Kani) (loVhada eLe yA gereyanunx oLagoMDa) AvaraNa shile; horashile. 
\num{7} (\pArxparx) (rasetxya kAluhAdiyalilx) goVDeya pakakx (caraMDiya pakakxvalalx). 
\num{8} rasetxya pakakx, badi (naDurasetxyalalx). 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{bang} (\engit{or} \eng{run) one's head against a (brick) wall} goVDege talebaDiduko; asAdhayxvAdadadxkekx parxyatinxsu, keYhacucx. 
\num{2} \eng{blank wall} bariya goVDe; KAli goVDe; kada, horabAgilu, kiTaki, \mo vu ilalxda yA alaMkaraNagaLilalxda goVDe. 
\num{3} \eng{(drive} \engit{or} \eng{send person) up the wall} (\AmA) (obabxnanunx) reVgisu, keraLisu, talekeDisu. 
\num{4} \eng{give (person) the wall} (obabxrigobabxru edurAdAga, obabxnige) goVDeya pakakxvanunx (eMdare hecucx nimaRlavU surakiSxtavU Ada pakakxvanunx) biTuTxkoDu. 
\num{5} \eng{go the wall} soVtu hoVgu yA mUle pAlAgu. 
\num{6} \eng{off the wall} (\ame) (\ashi) rUDhige virudadhxvAgi; saMparxdAyabadadhxvAgirade. 
\num{7} \eng{see through a brick wall} alwkikavAda, loVkoVtatxravAda -- oLagaNiNxru, aMtadaRqSiTx iru. 
\num{8} \eng{take the wall of} (obabxrigobabxru edurAdAga), obabxnige goVDeya pakakxvanunx biTuTxkoDadiru (eMdare aSuTx swjanayxvanUnx toVrisadiru). 
\num{9} \eng{the} \hyperlink{writing pagu(2)}{writing} \eng{on the wall.} 
\num{10} \eng{up the wall} (\AmA) roVSaveVri yA talekeTaTxMtAgi: \eng{went up the wall when he heard it} adanunx keVLidAga hucucxhucAcxda. 
\num{11} \eng{walls have ears} goVDegaLigU kivi ide; hoMci keVLuvavaru idAdxre yA irabahudu. 
\num{12} \eng{with one's} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{back(1) nuga(30)}{$^1$back} \eng{to the wall.} 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\pron{vAlfTuvAlf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (jamaKAnada \vi) goVDeyiMda goVDeyavaregina; koVNeya nelavanenxlalx mucucxva. 
\numi{2} (\AmA) 
\banum
\alnum{a} heVraLa; yatheVSaTx. 
\alnum{b} vAyxpaka; savaRtarx iruva: \eng{wall-to-wall pop music} savaRtarx vAyxpisiruva, elelxDegU haraDida pApf saMgiVta. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\expl{}

\num{2} (gotutxguri ilalxde) aleyutitxru; ODADutitxru; sutAtxDutitxru; tirugutitxru. 
\num{3} (hoLe, rasetx, vayxkitx, \mo vara \vi) sutitxbaLasi, aMkuDoMkAgi -- sAgu. 
\num{4} dAribiTuTx hoVgu; dAritapupx; nelebiTuTx ale. 
\numi{5} 
\banum

\bentry
\word[want(1)]{want} 
\pron{vAMTf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} kore(yAgiruvudu); korate; nUyxnate; rAhitayx; aBAva: \eng{the ship is rotting for want of paint} baNaNxvilalxde A haDagu koLeyutitxde. \eng{I took this for want of anything better} beVre utatxmavAda yAvudU ilalxda kAraNa nAnu idanunx hiDide. \eng{want of judgment} viveVcaneya korate yA aBAva. 
\num{2} Avashayxkate; agatayx; baDatana; dAridarxyX: \eng{he is in want of money} avanige haNada Avashayxkate ide, haNa agatayxvAgide. \eng{he is living in dire want} avanu kaDubaDatanadalilx badukutitxdAdxne. 
\num{3} (badukige, suKakekx, jayakekx, korateyAgiruvudara pUreYkege AvashayxkavAda vasutxvina) apeVkeSx; bayake; vAMCe yA bayasida vasutx: \eng{a man of few wants} hecucx apeVkeSxgaLilalxda vayxkitx. \eng{this meets a long-felt want} diVGaRkAladiMda anuBavisutitxdadx oMdu bayakeyanunx idu niVgisutatxde. \eng{I can supply your wants} nAnu ninanx agatayxgaLanunx pUreYsabalelx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[want(2)]{want} 
\pron{vAMTf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} ilalxdiru; aBAva hoMdiru; rahitavAgiru; korate, nUyxnate uLaLxdAdxgiru: \eng{the drawer wants a handle} arege hiDiyilalx. 
\num{2} iMtiSuTx koreyAgiru. 
\num{3} beVkAgiru; agatayxviru; AvashayxkavAgiru: \eng{he wants money} avanige haNa beVkAgide. \eng{it wants doing} adanunx mADabeVkAgide. 
\numi{4} 
\banum
\alnum{a} bayasu; apeVkiSxsu; paDeyalu iSaTxpaDu, iciPxsu: \eng{I want some sugar} nAnu savxlapx sakakxre bayasutetxVne. \eng{I want it done} adanunx mADabeVkeMdu nAnu apeVkiSxsutetxVne. \eng{I want you to try} niVnu parxyatinxsabeVkeMdu nAnu iciPxsutetxVne. 
\alnum{b} (\kanmu\ leYMgika BoVgakAkxgi vayxkitxyanunx) bayasu. 
\alnum{c} (\kanmu\ \birx) \kanmu\ nidiRSaTx riVtiya kAyaR bayasu, beVkAgiru: \eng{the garden wants weeding} toVTakekx kaLe kiVLabeVkAgide. 
\eanum

\emng

  \noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} korateyiru; aBAvaviru: \eng{let him want for nothing} avanige yAvudakUkx korateyilalxdirali. 
\num{2} (\ame, \AmA) (vayxvahAra, kirxye, \mo vugaLalilx) seVralu, toreyalu yA paDeyalu bayasu: \eng{I want to be out} nAnu toredu hoVga(lu) bayasutetxVne.

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{do not want to} 
\banum
\alnum{a} manasisxlalxdiru; iSaTxvilalxdiru. 
\alnum{b} mADalAgadu; mADabAradu: \eng{you don't want to overdo it} niVnu adanunx ati mADabAradu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{wanted (by the police)} (aparAdhiyeMdu gumAni iruva kAraNa) poliVsarige beVkAgidAdxne; poliVsaru (avananunx) huDukutitxdAdxre.

\bentry
\word[war(1)]{war} 
\pron{vArf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} yudadhx; samara; saMgArxma; kadana; kALaga; raNa: 
\banum
\alnum{a} rASaTxrXrASaTxrXgaLige yA oMdeV rASaTxrXdalilx pakaSxpakaSxgaLige shasAtxrXsatxrXgaLiMda naDeyuva hoVrATa. 
\alnum{b} yudadhxkAla; yudadhxda avadhi. 
\alnum{c} yudadhx parisithxti; aMtArASiTxrXVya shAsana \mo vanunx sathxgitagoLisuvike. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} (\rUpa) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxgaLu, guMpugaLu, \mo vugaLa naDuvaNa) vAyxjayx; jagaLa; kalaha; saPxdheR; tikAkxTa: \eng{war of words} vAguyxdadhx; mAtina jagaLa. 
\alnum{b} (aparAdha, baDatana, roVga, \mo vugaLa virudadhx) hoVrATa; samara; nililxsade naDesuva caLavaLi. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (\rUpa) neYsagiRka shakitxgaLa saMGaSaR. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{a good war} (\AmA) yudadhxda kAladalilx oMdu saMtoVSakaravAda avadhi. 
\num{2} \eng{a holy war} pavitarxyudadhx; dhamaRyudadhx; dhAmiRka kAraNakAkxgi mADuva yudadhx. 
\num{3} \eng{art of war} yudadhxkale; yudadhxsanAnxha taMtarxgaLu. 
\hyperdef{W}{war(1)pagu(4)}{} 
\num{4} \eng{at war} (shaturxgaLoDane) yudadhxdalilx toDagi, niratavAgi. 
\num{5} \eng{carry the war into the enemy's camp} (\engit{or} \eng{country)} (\rUpa) parxtidALi naDesu; keVvala AtamxrakaSxNeyalelxV taqpatxnAgade parxtAyxroVpa \mo vanunx mADu. 
\num{6} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{council pagu(3)}{council} \eng{of war.} 
\num{7} \eng{declare war} yAvudeV rASaTxrX(gaLa) meVle yA (\rUpa) (saMsethx, padadhxti, \mo vugaLa meVle) yudadhx GoVSisu. 
\num{8} \eng{dogs of war} (\kAparx) yudadhxda anAhuta, vinAsha. 
\num{9} \eng{go to war} yudadhx hUDu; hoVrATavanunx AraMBisu, upakarxmisu. 
\num{10} \eng{go to the wars} (\pArxparx) seYnikanAgu; seYnika vaqtitxge seVru. 
\num{11} \eng{have been in the wars} (\AmA) yudadhxda gAya, hoDeta, \mo vugaLa gurutugaLuLaLxvanAgiru. 
\num{12} \eng{laws of war} (shaturx kAyARcaraNege miti kalipxsalu nAgarika janAMgagaLu aMgiVkarisiruva) yudadhxniyamagaLu; yudadhxdhamaR. 
\numi{13} \eng{private war} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxgaLalilx yA kuTuMbagaLalilx, kole \mo vugaLa shAsanagaLanunx lekikxsade, naDeyuva) vayxkitxkalaha yA kuTuMbakalaha. 
\alnum{b} KAsagi yudadhx; beVroMdu rASaTxrXda nAgarikara meVle savxdeVshada sakARrada anumati ilalxde mADuva dALi, hoVrATa. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{14} \eng{rights of war} yudadhxda hakukxgaLu; shAMtikAladalilx anAyxyaveMdu gaNaneyAguva, Adare yudadhxkAladalilx yudadhxniratarige kelavu kAyaRgaLanunx mADalu anumati koDuva hakukxgaLu. 
\num{15} \eng{the War} Iga naDeyutitxruva yA ititxVcege mugida yudadhx. 
\num{16} \eng{trade of war} yudadhxda kasabau; seYnikavaqtitx. 
\num{17} \eng{war of} \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{attrition pagu}{attrition}. 
\num{18} \eng{war of the elements} (\kAparx) neYsagiRka shakitxgaLa saMGaSaR; birugALigaLu, parxvAhagaLu, BUkaMpagaLu, \mo\ anAhutagaLu. 
\hyperdef{W}{war(1) pagu(19)}{} 
\num{19} \eng{war of nerves} (edurALiya manaHsethxYyaRvanunx karxmakarxmavAgi hALumADuva) dhaqtigeVDi yudadhx; sethxYyaRnAshaka yudadhx. 
\num{20} \eng{Wars of the Roses} (\ca) yAkfR matutx laMkAsaTxrfgaLa naDuve, \eng{15}ne shatamAnadalilx iMgelxMDinalilx naDeda aMtayuRdadhx (biLi matutx keMpu gulAbigaLiMda parxtinidhisalapxTaTxdudx). 
\num{21} \eng{war to the knife} \kanmu\ vayxkitxvayxkitxgaLa naDuve kaTaTxkaDeyavaregU naDeyuva, nidARkiSxNayxvAda hoVrATa. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[warrant(1)]{warrant} 
\pron{vAraMTf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} adhikAra; AdhAra; parxmANa; samathaRne; yAvudeV kelasavanunx mADalu adhikAra koDuva vayxkitx yA viSaya: \eng{you have no warrant for this action} I kelasakekx ninage yAva AdhAravU ilalx, adhikAravU ilalx. \eng{his promise, or order is our strength, our warrant} avana vAgAdxna, yA apapxNe, namamx bala, namamx AdhAra. \eng{I will be your warrant} nAnu ninage AdhAravAgirutetxVne, adhikAra koDuvavanAgirutetxVne. \eng{with warrant of a good conscience} shudadhxvAda aMtasAsxkiSxya samathaRneyiMda. 
\numi{2} vAraMTu: 
\banum
\alnum{a} pAvati, salilxke -- patarx. 
\alnum{b} (haNavanunx paDedukoLaLxlu) liKita adhikAra patarx, apapxNe: \eng{dividend warrant} DiviDeMDanunx paDeyalu liKita adhikArapatarx. 
\alnum{c} sarakugaLanunx paDedukoLaLxlu yA odagisalu, seVvegaLanunx paDedukoLaLxlu yA odagisalu liKita adhikAra patarx, rahadAri: \eng{travel warrant} parxyANada rahadAri. 
\alnum{d} serehiDiyalu, mane, meY, \mo vanunx shoVdhisalu adhikAra patarx, rahadAri. 
\alnum{e} (mokadadxme hUDiruvavana parxtiyAgi kaTaTxLe naDesalu) vakAlatutxnAme; vakiVlanige koTiTxruva adhikArapatarx. 
\alnum{f} seVvAvadhiyiMda, seVvAvadhiya baladiMda, adhikArakekx baMdiruva adhikAriya adhikAra sAthxnada parxmANapatarx, saTiRphikeVTu.

\bentry
\word[wash(1)]{wash} 
\pron{vASf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (yAvudeV darxvadiMda, \kanmu\ niVriniMda muKa \mo vanunx, meYyanunx yA yAvudeV vasutxvanunx) toLe; cokakxTamADu; shucigoLisu; nimaRlagoLisu. 
\num{2} (\rUpa) parishudadhxgoLisu: \eng{wash me thoroughly from mine iniquity} nananx pApagaLanunx toLedu parishudadhxgoLisu. 
\num{3} (kale, koLe, \mo vanunx) toLeduhAku; toLedu hoVgalADisu. 
\num{4} keY, bAyi, \mo vanunx toLeduko. 
\num{5} toVyisu; neneyisu; AdarxRgoLisu; odedxmADu: \eng{roses washed with dew} ibabxniyiMda toyadx gulAbigaLu. 
\num{6} (nadi, samudarx, \mo vugaLa \vi) niVru (kare, daDa, tiVra, \mo vanunx) tAgu; baDi; toLe. 
\numi{7} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (calisutitxruva darxvada \vi) (hesarisida dikikxnalilx) kocicxkoMDu hoVgu; dUDikoMDu hoVgu: \eng{a wave washed him overboard} oMdu ale avananunx haDaginiMda (kaDalige) kocicxhAkitu. \eng{he was washed up by the sea} avanu samudarxdiMda meVlakekx (tiVrakekx) dUDalapxTaTx. 
\alnum{b} (samudarxda alegaLa \vi) baDi; apapxLisu; baDidu, apapxLisi -- sameyisu, koreduhAku: \eng{sea washed cliffs} samudarxda alegaLiMda sameduhoVda koVDugalulxgaLu. 
\alnum{c} toVDu; koreduhAku: \eng{water had washed a channel} niVru oMdu kAluveyanunx koreduhAkitutx, toVDitutx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} aduranunx -- toLe, jAlADu; niVriniMda toLedu aduriniMda loVhavanunx beVpaRDisu. 
\num{9} (kAgada, goVDe, \mo vugaLa meVle) teLuvAgi baNaNx -- baLi, toDe, savaru, leVpisu. 
\num{10} (kiVLuloVhagaLige cinanx \mo vugaLa) mulAmu -- hAku, leVpisu.

\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (muKa, keYbAyi) toLeduko. 
\num{2} (baTeTx) oge. 
\num{3} (niVru) jaLajaLane hari. 
\num{4} (niVrina \vi) seLedukoMDu, eLedukoMDu, sAgisikoMDu -- hoVgu. 
\num{5} (baTeTx yA baNaNxda \vi) toLedarU, ogedarU -- hoVgadiru yA hAniyAgadiru. 
\num{6} (kale \mo vugaLa \vi) ogetadiMda hoVgu; ogeyuvudariMda ilalxvAgu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{wash down} (\kanmu\ doDaDx meVlemxYyanunx yA vasutxvanunx) saMpUNaRvAgi toLe. 
\num{2} \eng{wash down with} (AhArada taruvAya) pAniVyavanunx kuDi yA seVvisu. 
\numi{3} \eng{washed out} 
\banum
\alnum{a} ogetadiMda malinavAda, kiSxVNavAda, mAsida. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) kiSxVNavAda; dubaRlagoMDa; dhaqtigeTaTx; edegeTaTx; dheYyaRguMdida.

\num{5} \eng{wash one's dirty} \hyperref{kandict_l.pdf}{L}{linen(1) nuga(1)}{$^1$linen} \eng{at home} (\engit{or} \eng{in public).} 
\num{6} \eng{wash one's hands} (\sw) shwcagaqhakekx hoVgu. 
\num{7} \eng{wash one's hands of} (yAvudeV oMdariMda) tananx hoNegArike, javAbAdxriyanunx koDaviko; keYtoLeduko(MDubiDu).

\bentry
\word[wash(2)]{wash} 
\pron{vASf} 
\gl{\nA}

\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} mAjaRna; toLeyuvudu yA toLeyalapxDuvudu; ogeyuvudu yA ogeyalapxDuvudu; toLeta; ogeta: \eng{give it a good wash} adanunx omemx cenAnxgi toLe, oge. \eng{I must get} (\engit{or} \eng{have) a wash} nAnu meY toLedukoLaLxbeVku, sAnxna mADabeVku. 
\num{2} ogeyabeVkAda, ogeyutitxruva baTeTxgaLu. 
\num{3} niVrina harivu yA sapapxLa (\kanmu\ niVrinalilx pAterxya yA haDagina calanadiMdAguva alegaLa sadudx). 
\num{4} (calisutitxruva vimAnada hiMdina) hiMgALi; raBasada gALi. 
\num{5} niVru kocicxkoMDu baMda mekakxlu (maNuNx). 
\num{6} (kaDalina iLitadalilx mAtarx goVcaravAguva) maraLina dibabx. 
\num{7} (haMdigaLige koDuva aDige maneya) kalagacucx matutx tiMduLida cUrupAru. 
\num{8} Asavanakekx muMce kiNavxnagoLuLxtitxruva mAlfTx \mo vu. 
\num{9} teLaLxneya, kiVLutarada -- sapepxya darxvAhAra: \eng{this soup, tea, claret is mere wash} I sAru, TiV, kAlxreTf(veYnu) bariya tiLiniVru. 
\num{10} kalagacucx; (pArxNigaLige koDuva) darxvAhAra. 
\num{11} (\rUpa) oNaharaTe; baudidhxhiVna mAtu; aviveVkada mAtu. 
\num{12} shucimADalu yA gAya, varxNa, \mo vanunx guNapaDisalu yA soVMku nivArisalu yA baNaNxhAkalu baLasuva darxva. 
\num{13} auSadhada loVSanf, dhAvaka, mAjaRka yA aMgarAga: \eng{eye wash} kaNiNxna loVSanf. 
\num{14} jalavaNaRda teLuvAda leVpana; goVDeya vaNaRleVpa yA loVhada leVpa. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{come out in the wash} 
\banum
\alnum{a} sapxSaTxvAgu. 
\alnum{b} kAlAnukarxmadalilx (toMdaregaLu) -- parihAravAgu, nivAraNeyAgu; taqpitxkaravAda, samapaRka sithxtige baru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{the wash} (doVbiKAneyalilx) caluve(mADuvudu): \eng{send the clothes to the wash} A baTeTxgaLanunx caluvege, caluvegAgi kaLuhisu. 
\enum

\gl{\gu}

\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (parxdeVsha \mo vugaLa \vi) (sAvxBAvikavAda kAraNagaLiMdaloV shaturxgaLa hAvaLiyiMdaloV pArxkaqtika anAhutagaLiMdaloV) pALubidadx; nijaRnavAda; beMgADAda; baMjarAda; maraLugADAda. 
\num{2} (\rUpa) Asakitxrahita; sAvxrasayxvilalxda; niVrasavAda: \eng{the waste periods of history} itihAsada niVrasavAda avadhigaLu. 
\num{3} AvashayxkategiMta miVrida; vayxthaRvAda; nirupayukatxvAda; baLasi mikukxhoVda. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} \eng{lie waste} vayxvasAyavilalxde bididxru. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry

\expl{}
\bmng

\num{2} kaLape kAgadadaMte kANu. 
\num{3} vayxthaRvAgi KacuR mADu; poVlumADu; sAkaSuTx parxtiPalavilalxde vayxyamADu; duMdu mADu: \eng{waste time} kAla vayxthaRmADu. \eng{waste money} haNavanunx poVlumADu. \eng{waste food} AhAravanunx vayxthaRmADu. 
\num{4} (obabxnige baudidhxvAda \mo vanunx) vayxthaRvAgi koDu; vayxthaRvAgi mAtanADu; yAvudeV pariNAma uMTumADade mAtanADu, baudidhxvAda \mo vanunx heVLu. 
\num{5} (karxmeVNa) samesu; shakitxhiVnagoLisu; dubaRlagoLisu; kiSxVNagoLisu; satatxvXkaLe: \eng{his resources were wasted} avana shakitxyelalx kaLeduhoVyitu.

\bentry
\word[watch(1)]{watch} 
\pron{vAcf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} 
\banum
\alnum{a} rAtirx ecacxrada kAla; jAgaraNe. 
\alnum{b} parxhara; pArxciVna kAladalilx rAtirxyanunx viBAgisutitxdadx avadhigaLalilx oMdu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} ecacxrike; ecacxra; ecacxradiMda noVDutatx, kAyutatx iruvudu; eDebiDade, saMtatavAgi -- gamanisutitxruvudu: \eng{keep (a) watch} ecacxradiMda kAyu, kAvaliru. \eng{keep (a) good watch} cenAnxgi kAyu; eveyikakxde kAyu. 
\num{3} (\ca) rAtirx kAvalinavanu yA kAvaludaLa, pahareyavanu yA pahare daLa; rAtirxya veVLeyalilx biVdigaLalilx gasutx tiruguvavanu yA gasutx tiruguva paDe. 
\num{4} (\ca) (\eng{18}neya shatamAnadalilx seVnege seVrada) heYlAYxMDf paDe. 
\num{5} (haDagina meVle) (nAlukx gaMTegaLa) kelasada veVLe, saradi. 
\numi{6} (\nw) 
\banum
\alnum{a} payARya daLa; oMdAda meVloMdaraMte, kelasa mADalu nAvika daLavanunx viBAgisiruva eraDu daLagaLalolxMdu. 
\alnum{b} nAlukx gaMTegaLa avadhiya nigadita kelasa. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{7} keYgaDiyAra yA jeVbinalilxTuTxkoLuLxva cikakx gaDiyAra. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{be on the watch} (\sA\ niriVkiSxsutitxruva yA bayasutitxruva yA aMjutitxruva GaTanegAgi) kAyutitxru; eduru noVDutitxru. 
\num{2} \eng{in the watches of the night} rAtirxya jAgarada avadhigaLalilx oMdu: \eng{the ghost appears in the fourth watch of the night} rAtirxya nAlakxneV jAgaradalilx A perxVtavu kANisikoLuLxtatxde. 
\numi{3} \eng{pass as a watch in the night} 
\banum
\alnum{a} rAtirxya oMdu jAgaradaMte kaLeduhoVgu 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) beVga maretu hoVgu; shiVGarxvAgi samxqqtiyiMda mareyAgu 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{set(1) pagu(10)}{$^1$set} \eng{a (or the) watch.} 
\num{5} \eng{star board and port watch} (haDaginalilx saradiya meVle kelasa mADabeVkAda) balanAvika daLa, eDanAvika daLa. 
\num{6} \eng{watch below} biDuvu (kAla, veVLe). 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[watch(2)]{watch} 
\pron{vAcf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (vayxkitx \mo vara meVle) kaNiNxTiTxru; daqSiTx iTiTxru; kAvaliDu; ecacxradiMda noVDu; gamanisu: \eng{they had him watched by detectives} avaru avana meVle patetxVdArara kAvaliTiTxdadxru. \eng{I was watching television} nAnu gamanaviTuTx dUradashaRnavanunx noVDutitxdedx. \eng{the boy was paid to watch sheep} A huDuganige kurigaLanunx kAyalu veVtana koDalAgutitxtutx. \eng{I shall watch your career with interest} nAnu ninanx puroVBivaqdidhxyanunx AsakitxyiMda gamanisutitxruvenu. \eng{I have to watch my weight} nAnu nananx tUkavanunx (hecacxdaMte) noVDikoLaLxbeVkAgide. 
\num{2} avakAshakAkxgi (samaya) kAyutitxru. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} ecacxravAgiru; jAgarUkanAgiru; huSArAgiru; oLeLxya avakAsha \mo vudakAkxgi gamanaviTuTx kAyutitxru. 
\num{2} kAvaliru; pahare iru; yAvudanenxV kApADalu gamanaviTuTx noVDutitxru. 
\num{3} (\pArxparx) (pArxthaRne \mo\ dhAmiRka kirxyegAgi) ecacxravAgiru; jAgaraNemADu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{watched pot never boils} kaLavaLadiMda kAyutitxdadxre kAla ati diVGaRvenisutatxde. 
\num{2} \eng{watch it (or oneself)} ecacxravAgiru; munenxcacxrike vahisu. 
\num{3} \eng{watch one's chance} avakAshakAkxgi samaya kAyutitxru. \eng{} 
\numi{4} \eng{watch one's step} (\AmA) 
\banum
\alnum{a} noVDi hejejxyiDu; mugagxrisadaMte ecacxravAgiru. 
\alnum{b} hejejx gamanisu; tapupx mADadaMte ecacxravAgiru; ninanx tapipxniMda beVrobabxnige saMdhAna \mo vugaLalilx anukUlavAgadaMte jAgarUkanAgiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{5} \eng{watch out} (\engit{or} \eng{for)} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (AkarxmaNa, akasAmxtf GaTane, \mo vanunx edurisalu) tananx huSArinalilx, ecacxrikeyiMda iru. 
\alnum{b} (apAyasUcaneyAgi) ecacxrikeyiMdiru; huSAru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{watch the} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{clock(1)nuga(6)}{$^1$clock}.

\emng

\num{1} (rAjakiVya pakaSxda tatatxvXgaLanunx saMkeSxVpavAgi sUcisuva) sUtarx; mAtu; udAgxra; GoVSaNe, \udA\ \eng{equal pay for equal work} sarisamanAda kelasakekx sarisamanAda veVtana. 
\num{2} (\ca) (seYnayx) saMkeVtapada; gurutu mAtu; seYnayxkekx yA AyA paDege mAtarx tiLiyuva guTuTxmAtu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[water(1)]{water} 
\pron{vATarf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} niVru; jala; vAri; paya; udaka; aMbau; shara: 
\banum
\alnum{a} pAradashaRkavAda, vAsaneyilalxda, ruciyilalxda (Akisxjanf matutx heYDorxjanfgaLa) darxvasaMyukatx (rAsAyanika sUtarx, \eng{$\bg\rm H\eg_2\bg\rm O\eg$}). 
\alnum{b} samudarx, saroVvara, nadi, maLegaLa matutx jiVvigaLu sarxvisuva, jalAMshaviruva darxva. 
\alnum{c} (samudarx, nadi, saroVvara, \mo) niVru; niVrina haravu; jalarAshi. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\bava dalilx) jalaBAga; jala parxdeVsha; samudarxda yA nadiya BAga: \eng{in Icelandic waters} aisfleMDina jalaBAgadalilx. 
\num{3} (aneVkaveVLe \eng{the waters}) (Kanijajalada UTe \mo vugaLalilxna) Kanija jala. 
\num{4} oMdu nidiRSaTx vasutxvina dArxvaNa: \eng{lavender water} lAYxveMDarf dArxvaNa. 
\num{5} (vajarx \mo vugaLa \vi) niVru; pAradashaRkate matutx ujajxvXlate. 
\num{6} darxva baMDavALa; SeVru hecacxLadiMda keYgArike yA vANijayx saMsethxya nAmamAtarx baMDavALavanunx hecicxsuvudariMda seVrida baMDavALada motatx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{by water} jalamAgaRvAgi; haDagu \mo vugaLa mUlaka. 
\num{2} \eng{cast one's bread upon the waters} kaqtajacnxteyanAnxgali parxtiPalavanAnxgali bayasade satakxmaR mADu. 
\num{3} \eng{in deep water(s)} kaSaTxgaLalilx toLalutatx; saMkaTakekx sikikx. 
\numi{4} \eng{make water} 
\banum
\alnum{a} mUtarxvisajiRsu. 
\alnum{b} (haDagina \vi) niVru oLakekx nugugx yA horakekx soVru. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{5} \eng{of the first water} 
\banum
\alnum{a} atuyxtatxma, atuyxtakxqqSaTx -- guNada: \eng{diamond of the first water} atuyxtakxqqSaTx vajarx. \eng{genius of the first water} savaRsherxVSaThx parxtiBe. 
\alnum{b} (\hiV) atayxMta kiVLAda; heVyavAda: \eng{blunder of the the first water} atayxMta heVyavAda tapupx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{on the water} (\rUpa) doVNiyalilx yA haDaginalilx. 
\num{7} \eng{pass water} mUtarxvisajiRsu. 
\hyperdef{W}{water(1) pagu(8)}{} 
\num{8} \eng{pour} (\engit{or} \eng{throw) cold water on} taNiNxVreracu; yoVjane \mo vanunx hiVyALisi nirutAsxhagoLisu; vayxkitxyanunx nirutAsxhagoLisu. 
\num{9} \eng{shed blood like water} rakatxvanunx niVrinaMte celulx; dayAdAkiSxNayxvilalxde kolulx. 
\num{10} \eng{spend money like water} haNavanunx niVrinaMte celulx; dhArALavAgi, pariNAmavanunx lekikxsade vecacxmADu. 
\num{11} \eng{water of life} AdhAyxtimxka jAcnxna. 
\num{12} \eng{waters of forgetfulness} visamxqqti yA maraNa. 
\num{13} \eng{water under the bridge} \engit{or} \eng{over the dam} maraLi bArada gatakAla; kaLeduhoVda matutx matetx saripaDisalAgada GaTanegaLu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\expl{}

\bentry
\word[water(3)]{water} 
\pron{vATarf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} niVru cimukisu; niVriniMda odedxmADu. 
\num{2} (giDagaLu \mo vakekx) niVranunx -- hAku, koDu. 
\num{3} (hAlu, biyarf, \mo vakekx) niVranunx berasu, beresi teLavu mADu. 
\num{4} (nadi \mo vugaLa \vi, oMdu sathxLakekx) niVranunx odagisu; dorakisikoDu. 
\num{5} (pArxNige) niVriDu; niVranunx kuDisu. 
\num{6} (\kanmu\ \BUkaq dalilx) tereyiDisu; aleya AkAra uMTumADu; tayArisuvAga teVvamADi, otatxDakekx oLapaDisi, baTeTxya meVle alalxlelxV tereya AkAra uMTumADu: \eng{watered silk} tereyiDisida reVSemx. 
\num{7} (haNakAsina \vi) kaMpaniya Asitxge EnanUnx seVrisade, (eMdare kaMpaniya nijavAda baMDavALavanunx hecicxsade) hosa SeVrugaLanunx mAruvudara mUlaka kaMpaniya nAmamAtarx baMDavALavanunx hecicxsu (eMdare kaMpaniya sAlada horeyanunx hecicxsu).

\num{2} (haDagu, eMjinu, \mo vugaLa yA avanunx noVDikoLuLxvavana \vi) niVranunx tuMbiko; BatiRmADiko. 
\num{3} (uriyutitxruva kaNuNxgaLa \vi) kaNiNxVru osaru, soVru, suri. 
\num{4} (AhAravanunx kaMDAga yA AhAravanunx yA iSaTxvAdadadxnunx niriVkiSxsuvAga bAyiya \vi) niVrUru; jolulx surisu.

\bentry
\word[way(1)]{way} 
\pron{veV} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (ODADuva yA yAvudeV sathxLakekx hoVguva) rasetx; dAri; mAgaR; patha (\rUpa\ saha): \eng{asked the way to Mysore} meYsUrige hoVguva dAri keVLida. 
\num{2} (kaTaTxDa \mo vugaLa oLakekx hoVguva yA Acege hoVguva) dAri: \eng{could not find the way out} horakekx hoVguva dAri kANalilalx, sigalilalx. 
\num{3} (udedxVshavoMdanunx sAdhisuva) vidhAna; karxma; riVti; yoVjane; upAya: \eng{this is not the way to do it} adanunx mADuva vidhAna idalalx. \eng{there is a right way and a wrong way of using the tool} upakaraNavanunx baLasuva sariyAda riVti oMdide, tapu px riVti oMdide. \eng{do it this way} adanunx hiVge, I riVti mADu. 
\num{4} sAdhakashakitx; obabxna udedxVshavanunx pUreYsuva, guriyanunx sAdhisuva sAmathaRyx: \eng{he has a way with him} avanalolxMdu visheVSa sAmathaRyxvide. 
\num{5} vayxkitxyobabxnige iSaTxvAda, avanu bayasida yA Ayekx mADida -- kAyaRvidhAna, kAyaRriVti, mAgaR. 
\num{6} padadhxti; vADike; rUDhi; aBAyxsa; vataRne; naDevaLi; havAyxsa; veYyakitxka veYlakaSxNayx: \eng{has a way of forgetting things} viSayagaLanunx maretubiDuva aBAyxsavide. \eng{it is not my way to deceive people} janaranunx vaMcisuvudu nananx padadhxtiyalalx. \eng{things had a way of going badly} parisithxtigaLu keTuTxhoVguvudu oMdu vADikeyAgitutx. \eng{he has a way of leaving the bills unpaid} bilulxgaLanunx pAvati mADadiruvudu avanadoMdu rUDhi. 
\num{7} nidiRSaTx jiVvanakarxma yA nidiRSaTx kAyaRvidhAna: \eng{I soon got into his ways} nAnu beVga avana jiVvanakarxmagaLanunx aritukoMDe. \eng{soon got into the way of it} beVga adara kAyaRvidhAnagaLanunx kaMDukoMDe. 
\num{8} GaTanegaLu saMBavisuva sahaja -- karxma, riVti: \eng{that is always the way} GaTanegaLu saMBavisuvudu yAvAgalU aMteyeV, adeV riVtiyalilxyeV. 
\num{9} parxyANa dUra; parxyANa mADida yA mADabeVkAda dUra: \eng{is a long way away} bahaLa dUradalilxde. 
\num{10} (muMduvareyalu) nirAtaMkavAda, aDiDxaDacaNegaLilalxda -- avakAsha, dAri. 
\num{11} aDacaNegaLilalxda -- eDe, jAga. 
\num{12} parxgatipatha; muMduvareyalu bayasuva yA sahajavAda -- mAgaR, parxdeVsha. 
\num{13} (yAvudeV dikikxnalilx) munanxDe; muMduvarike; parxgati: \eng{pushed my way through} nugigx dArimADikoMDu hoVde. \eng{fight one's way through} hoVrADutAtx oMdu sathxLada mUlaka hoVgu. 
\num{14} (haDagu \mo vugaLa) calana; karxmaNa; yAna; sAguvike: \eng{gather way} muMde yA veVgavAgi sAgu. \eng{lose way} nidhAnavAgi sAgu; veVga tagigxsu. 
\numi{15} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (sathxLadiMda sathxLakekx) parxyANa; hoVgutitxruvudu: \eng{met him on the way home} manege hiMdirugutitxdAdxga dAriyalilx kaMDe. 
\alnum{b} parxyANakAla; parxyANadalilx kaLeda yA kaLeyuva kAla: \eng{with songs to cheer the way} parxyANa mADutAtx ulAlxsadiMdiralu hADugaLanunx hADutatx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{16} nidiRSaTx dikukx; hesarisida kaDe: \eng{step this way} I kaDe bA. \eng{which way are you going?} elilxge, yAva kaDege hoVgutitxdidxVye? 
\num{17} (\bava dalilx) vasutxvoMdanunx oDeyabahudAda -- BAgagaLu, viBAgagaLu: \eng{split it three ways} adanunx mUru BAgagaLAgi oDe. 
\num{18} (\AmA) yAvudaradeV -- vAyxpitx, keSxVtarx: \eng{want a few things in the stationery way} leVKanasAmagirxgaLige saMbaMdhisida kelavu vasutxgaLu beVku. 
\num{19} (vayxkitxya) kasubau; vaqtitx; udoyxVga. 
\num{20} nidiRSaTx -- sithxti, parisithxti, avasethx, vidayxmAna: \eng{things are in a bad way} parisithxti keTaTxdAgide; vidayxmAnagaLu duHsithxtiyalilxve. 
\num{21} aMsha; viSaya; guNa: \eng{is useful in some ways} kelavu aMshagaLalilx upayukatxvAgide. 
\numi{22} (\bava dalilx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (hosa haDaganunx samudarxkekx iLisalu tolegaLu \mo vugaLiMda racisida) jAruhAdi; iLAlu; iLakalu. 
\alnum{b} yaMtarxvoMdanunx sarisalu baLasuva joVDikaMbi hAdi, mAgaR, \mo vu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{across} (\engit{or} \eng{over) the way} edurina; edurubadiya; (\kanmu\ rasetxya) eduruBAgadalilxna: \eng{house across} (\engit{or} \eng{over) the way} edurumane; edurubadiya mane. 
\hyperdef{W}{way(1)pagu(2)}{} 
\num{2} \eng{all the way} iDiV dUra; pUtiRyAgi. 
\num{3} \eng{any way} = \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{anyway(1)}{anyway}. 
\num{4} \eng{be on one's way} horaDu; dAri hiDi; horaTuhoVgu; nigaRmisu. 
\numi{5} \eng{by the way} 
\banum
\alnum{a} pArxsaMgikavAgi; saMbaMdhisirada mAtanunx ADuvAga ADuva mAtAgi. 
\alnum{b} parxyANadalilx. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{6} \eng{by way of} 
\banum
\alnum{a} mUlaka; mAgaRvAgi: \eng{by way of Bangalore} beMgaLUrina mUlaka. 
\alnum{b} adakekx badalAgi, parxtiyAgi; A rUpadalilx: \eng{carries a stick by way of a weapon} Ayudhakekx badalAgi koVlanunx hiDididAdxne. \eng{did it by way of apology} kaSxmAyAcaneya rUpadalilx adanunx mADida. 
\alnum{c} udedxVshadiMda: \eng{by way of discovering the truth} nijAMshavanunx kaMDuhiDiyuva udedxVshadiMda. 
\alnum{d} kalipxsikoMDu yA toVpaRDisikoLuLxtatx: \eng{by way of making a great effort} BAri parxyatanxvanunx mADutitxruvaMte kalipxsikoMDu yA toVrisikoLuLxtatx. 
\alnum{e} mUlaka; muKAMtara; A riVtiyalilx, vidhAnadalilx. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{7} \eng{clear the way} 
\banum
\alnum{a} aDetaDegaLanunx tegeduhAku; dAri sugamagoLisu. 
\alnum{b} dAri biDu; pakakxkekx sari; saridu nilulx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} \eng{come one's way} obabxna pAlige baru; obabxnige -- sigu, laBayxvAgu 
\num{9} \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{feel(1) nuga(4)}{$^1$feel} \eng{one's way.} 
\num{10} \eng{find a way} dAri kaMDuko; guri sAdhisuva mAgaRvanunx, udedxVshasAdhaneya upAyavanunx kaMDuko. 
\num{11} \eng{find its} (\engit{or} \eng{the} \engit{or} \eng{one's) way} guri muTuTx; udidxSaTxsAthxna talupu. 
\num{12} \eng{either way} eraDaralilx yAvudAdarU oMdu riVtiyalilx; hiVgoVhAgoV; hiVgAdarU hAgAdarU. 
\hypertarget{way pagu13}{} 
\num{13} \eng{get} (\engit{or} \eng{have) one's way} tanage beVkenisidadxnunx paDeduko; tananx udedxVsha sAdhisuvaMte, iSATxthaR neraveVruvaMte noVDiko. 
\numi{14} \eng{give way} 
\banum
\alnum{a} taDeyalAradAgu; edurisalAgade hoVgu; maNi; bagugx. 
\alnum{b} (beVrobabxnige) dAribiDu; eDekoDu; Adayxte, parxthamAvakAsha koDu. 
\alnum{c} riyAyiti toVrisu, niVDu. 
\alnum{d} (kaTaTxDa \mo vugaLa \vi) meVlina BAradiMda -- kusi; muridu biVLu, bidudxhoVgu. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{15} \eng{give way to} 
\banum
\alnum{a} tananx sAthxnavanunx (beVrobabxnige yA beVroMdakekx) biTuTxkoDu. 
\alnum{b} (beVrobabx yA beVroMdu) tanagiMta meVlina sAthxnakekx EruvaMte Agu; tanagiMta meVlina sAthxnavanunx (inonxbabxnige yA inonxMdakekx) biTuTxkoDu. 
\alnum{c} (BAva \mo vugaLige) vashavAgu; sharaNAgu; sAvxdhiVnavAgu. 
\alnum{d} (aMbigara \vi) birusAgi huTuTx hAku. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{16} \eng{go a person's way} obabxnu hoVgutitxruva dikikxgeV, eDegeV hoVgu; obabxna jote, obabxnoDane hoVgu: \eng{are you going my way ?} niVnu nanonxDane, nAnu hoVgutitxruvalilxgeV hoVgutitxdidxVyA? 
\numi{17} \eng{go one's way} 
\banum
\alnum{a} horaDu; horaTuhoVgu; nigaRmisu. 
\alnum{b} (GaTanegaLu, saMdaBaRgaLu, parisithxtigaLu, \mo vugaLa \vi) (obabxnige) anukUl(kara)vAgiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{18} \eng{go one's own way} (\kanmu\ itarara salahe, baudidhxvAda, \mo vanunx lekikxsade, avugaLige virudadhxvAgi) tananxdeV dAri hiDi; tanage toVridaMteyeV mADu; savxtaMtarxvAgi vatiRsu. 
\num{19} \eng{go out of one's way} (yAvudanenxV sAdhisalu, neraveVrisalu) visheVSa parxyatanx mADu; rUDhiyAgiruvudakikxMta hecicxna mutuvajiR, parisharxma vahisu; yAvudeV kAraNa yA balavaMta ilalxde savxMta iceCxyiMda vatiRsu: \eng{went out of their way to help} sahAya mADalu visheVSa sharxmavahisidaru. 
\num{20} \eng{go the way of all good things} oLeLxya vasutxgaLaMte anivAyaRvAgi aLi, nAshavAgu. 
\num{21} \eng{go the way of all earth} (\engit{or} \eng{flesh} \engit{or} \eng{nature)} sAyu. 
\num{22} \eng{go the whole} (\engit{or} \eng{all the) way} (\AmA) pUtiR saMBoVga, pUNaRmeYthuna naDesu. 
\num{23} \eng{have a way} (yAvudanenxV mADalu) visheVSa kwshala yA sAmathaRyx hoMdiru. 
\num{24} \eng{have a way with one} AkaSaRka matutx olisuva guNa, riVtiniVti hoMdiru. 
\num{25} \eng{have one's way with} (\hA) yAroDaneyAdarU saMBoVga naDesu (\kanmu\ avara iSaTxkekx viroVdhavAgi eMba sUcaneyoDane). 
\num{26} \eng{have it} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{both(1) nuga(2)}{$^1$both} \eng{ways.} 
\num{27} \eng{have it one's own way} = \hyperlink{way pagu13}{?pagu? \((13)\)}. 
\num{28} \eng{have it your (own) way} (heVLidadxkekx yA sUcisidadxkekx olalxda manasisxna opipxgeya utatxravAgi) niVnu heVLidaMteyeV Agali; ninage toVridaMte mADu; nininxSaTx(daMte mADu). 
\num{29} \eng{in a} (\engit{or} \eng{one) way} (\engit{or} \eng{some ways)} savxlapxmaTiTxge; tusu. 
\num{30} \eng{in a} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{big(1) nuga(3)}{$^1$big} \eng{way.} 
\num{31} \eng{in a} \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{fair(1) nuga(8)}{$^1$fair} \eng{way.} 
\num{32} \eng{in a} (\engit{or} \eng{the}) \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{family(1) nuga(1)}{$^1$family} \eng{way.} 
\num{33} \eng{in a small way} saNaNx parxmANadalilx; mahatAvxkAMkeSx ilalxde. 
\num{34} \eng{in its way} adara riVtiyalilx; adakekx takukxdAda nidiRSaTx daqSiTxkoVnadiMda noVDidare.

\bentry
\word[wear(1)]{wear} 
\pron{veVrf} 
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ \eng{wore} \ucAcx\ voVrf; \BUkaq\ \eng{worn} \ucAcx\ voVnfR).}
\bmng
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (uDige, ABaraNagaLanunx) uDu; toDu; uTuTxko; toTuTxko; hAku; hAkiko; dharisu: \eng{wears green shorts} hasiru caDiDxyanunx uDutAtxne. \eng{she intends to wear earrings} avaLu OlegaLanunx dharisalu iciPxsutAtxLe. 
\num{2} sAmAnayxvAgi, vADikeyAgi -- uDu, toDu: \eng{wears green} hasirubaTeTx uDutAtxne. 
\num{3} (deVhada meVle uDupinaMte yA aMgadaMte) dharisu; hAkiko; toDu: \eng{wear a beard} gaDaDx biDu, beLesu. \eng{wear glasses} kananxDaka hAkiko. \eng{wear hair long} talegUdalanunx udadxvAgi iTuTxko. 
\num{4} (muKaBAva yA rUpavanunx) taLe; tALu; toVru; parxdashiRsu; parxkaTisu: \eng{wore a frown} siDukumoVre hAkidadx. \eng{wear a joyful face} saMtoVSada muKatoVru. \eng{wear a sour look} kahimoVre hAku. \eng{the day wore a different aspect} dina BinanxmuKa toTiTxtutx. 
\num{5} (\birx)(\AmA)(\sA\ niSeVdhavAciyoDane) opupx; sahisu; tALiko: \eng{they won't wear that excuse} avaru A sabaUbanunx opupxvudilalx. 
\num{6} ujijx, otAtxya heVri yA baLasi yAvudaradeV meVlemxYyanunx - hAnigoLisu, hALumADu, tUtubiVLisu, jiVNaRgoLisu, kaqshagoLisu yA BAgashaH aLisihAku: \eng{inscription has been worn} shAsana aLisihoVgide. \eng{wear one's trousers into holes} (\engit{or} \eng{bagginess)} -- SarAyiyanunx uTuTxuTuTx tUtu biVLisu (yA dagale mADu). \eng{worn to a stick with care} ciMteyiMda kaqshavAgi kaDiDxyAgidAdxne. \eng{toil-worn} duDimeyiMda biVLAgidAdxne. 
\num{7} saveyisu; teVyu; ujijxhAku: \eng{steps worn with pilgrims' feet} yAtirxkara kAlugaLiMda saveduhoVda meTiTxlugaLu. 
\num{8} susutx biVLisu; AyAsagoLisu; daNisu; baLalisu. 
\num{9} paTuTxhiDidu -- aDagisu; adumihAku; damanamADu; hosaki hAku: \eng{wear down opposition} viroVdhavanunx, parxtiBaTaneyanunx aDagisu, damanamADu. 
\num{10} (kAlavanunx) nidhAnavAgi kaLe. 
\num{11} (haDagina \vi) bAvuTa hArisu. 
\num{12} (\sA\ niVru \mo vugaLa \vi) savesi, koredu (tUtu, kAluve, \mo vanunx) mADu; koredu hAku. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} (otatxDa, ujujxvike yA baLakeyiMda) 
\banum
\alnum{a} samedu hoVgu; teVyu; jiVNaRvAgu; kaqshavAgu; kaSxyisu: \eng{the stick has worn down to a stump} koVlu samedu hoVgi moVTAgide. \eng{trousers have been worn out} SarAyi (baLakeyiMda) jiVNaRvAgide. 
\alnum{b} samedu, aLisi, ujijx -- hoVgu: \eng{the inscription has worn away} shAsana samedu hoVgide. \eng{the impression soon wore off} A aBipArxya beVga aLidu hoVyitu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} baLalihoVgu; daNi, susAtxgu. 
\num{3} bALu; bALike baru; sadayxda sithxtiyalilx yA kAyARcaraNe mADutAtx nidiRSaTx avadhiyavarege uLidiru. 
\num{4} (kAlada \vi) nidhAnavAgi -- sari, sAgu, kaLe. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{wear in one's heart} vayxkitxge yA tatatx vxkekx niSaThxnAgiru. 
\num{2} \eng{wear off} parxBAva yA tiVvarxte kuMdu, kaLeduko. 
\num{3} \eng{wear (one's years) well} (\AmA) vayasAsxgidadxrU yuvakanAgiyeV kANu.

\numie

\alnum{b} hutAtamxnAgiru.

\numie

\num{9} \eng{wear the trousers} dAMpatayxjiVvanadalilx meVlugeY, ALuva, parxdhAna -- pAtarxvAgiru. 
\num{10} \eng{wear the willow} BaganxperxVmiyAgiru. 
\num{11} \eng{wear thin} (tALemx \mo vugaLa \vi) kaDameyAgalu, (sabaUbau \mo vugaLa \vi) naMbike keDalu -- pArxraMBavAgu. 
\num{12} \eng{wear through the day} (parisithxti \mo vugaLiMda) heVgoV (niBAyisi) -- pArAgu, bacAvAgu. 
\numi{13} \eng{(well-)worn} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (hAsoyxVkitxgaLa \vi) haLasalAda; savakalAda. 
\alnum{b} (baTeTxbaregaLa \vi) baLasi jiVNaRvAda. 
\eanum
\numie

\banum
\alnum{a} uTaTx uDige; omemxyAdarU hAkikoMDa baTeTxbaregaLu; baLasida baTeTxbare. 
\alnum{b} (baLasi baLasi) jiVNaRvAda baTeTxbare.

\emng

\bentry
\word[weather(1)]{weather} 
\pron{vedarf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
havA; havAmAna; vAyuguNa; oMdu sathxLadalilx, oMdu kAladalilx yAvudeV parxdeVshadalilxruva vAyumaMDalada, vAtAvaraNada parisithxti: \eng{favourable weather} anukUlakaravAda have. \eng{seasonable weather} hitavAda have. \eng{good weather} oLeLxya, utatxma -- have. \eng{bad weather} keTaTx havA. \eng{cold weather} caLi have. \eng{dull weather} maMkAda, beVsara huTiTxsuva havA. \eng{rainy weather} maLeya vAtAvaraNa. \eng{windy weather} birugALiya havA. \eng{he goes out in all weathers} elalx bageya havegaLalUlx avanu horage saMcarisutAtxne. 
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{above the weather} (vimAnayAna) moVDagaLiMdAce shAMtavAda parxdeVshadalilx. 
\num{2} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{clerk(1) pagu(3)}{$^1$clerk} \eng{of the weather.} 
\num{3} \eng{keep a} (\engit{or} \eng{one's) weather eye open} ecacxradiMdiru; jAgarUkanAgiru. 
\num{4} \eng{make a good} (\engit{or} \eng{bad) weather of it} (\nw) birugALiyalilx cenAnxgi (yA keTaTxdAgi)vatiRsu, naDe. 
\num{5} \eng{make heavy weather} (samaseyx, kAyARcaraNe, \mo vugaLa) toMdareyanunx, kaSaTxsAdhayxteyanunx atishayisu; yAvudanenxV Agali tiVra kaSaTxveMdu dUru, goVLADu. 
\num{6} \eng{under stress of weather} birugALi \mo vugaLa kAraNadiMda. 
\hyperdef{W}{weather(1) pagu(7)}{} 
\num{7} \eng{under the weather} (\AmA) asavxsathxvAgiru; meY sariyilalxdiru yA manasusx samAdhAna sithxtiyalilxlalxdiru, parxkuSxbadhxvAgiru. 
\enum
\emng

\num{4} jAla; (\kanmu\ IjuhakikxgaLa matutx bAvaligaLa) kAlaberaLugaLa naDuve iruva camaRda pore; saMbaMdhaka, aMgAMsha -- pore.

\num{6} (\kanmu\ vaqtatxpatirxkeya mudarxNadalilx baLasuva) kAgadada doDaDx suruLi. 
\num{7} (yaMtarxgaLu \mo vugaLalilx GanaBAgagaLanunx kUDisuva, teLuvAda, capapxTeya) tagaDu; Palaka, \udA\ reYlubaMDiya gAliya guMBakUkx aMcigU (paTeTxgU) naDuvaNa tagaDu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}

\bentry
\word{week} 
\pron{viVkf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\sA\ shanivAra -- BAnuvAra naDurAtirxyiMda lekakx mADuva) vAra; ELudina(gaLa avadhi); sapAtxha. 
\num{2} vAra; yAvudeV dinadiMda gaNisida ELudinagaLu: \eng{can you come to us for a week} niVnu oMdu vAra kAla namamxlilxge barabalelxyA? 
\num{3} (\bava dalilx) diVGaRkAla; vAragaTaTxle: \eng{I have not seen you for weeks} ninanxnunx nAnu vAragaLagaTaTxLe kaMDilalx. \eng{I did it weeks ago} nAnu adanunx kelavu vAragaLa hiMdeyeV mADide. 
\numi{4} vAra: 
\banum
\alnum{a} soVmavAradiMda shukarxvAradavaregina aidu dinagaLu. 
\alnum{b} oMdu BAnuvArakUkx inonxMdu BAnuvArakUkx naDuvaNa Aru dinagaLu: \eng{I never go there in the week} vArada naDuve nAnu alilxge hoVguvudeV ilalx. 
\alnum{c} I avadhiyalilx mADida kelasada avadhi: \eng{42-hour week} nalavatetxraDu GaMTegaLa kAyARvadhi, vAra. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{a week} parxti vAra. 
\num{2} \eng{a week (from) today} (\engit{or} \eng{this day)} iMdiniMda oMdu vAra modalu yA taruvAya. 
\num{3} \eng{day of the week} vArada dina, \udA\ \eng{Monday, Tuesday,} itAyxdi. 
\num{4} \hyperref{kandict_k.pdf}{K}{knock(1) nuga(3)}{$^1$knock} \eng{one into the middle of next week.} 
\num{5} \eng{Monday week} muMdina soVmavAra. 
\num{6} \eng{today week} muMdina vAra I dina. 
\num{7} \eng{week of Sundays}, (\engit{or} \eng{weeks)} ELuvAragaLu, tuMba diVGARvadhi. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[weight(1)]{weight} 
\pron{veVTf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} tUka:

\alnum{b} beVre yAvudeV AkaSaRNa keVMdarxda dikikxnalilx kAyavu anuBavisuva AkaSaRNa bala. 
\alnum{c} kAyada guNa eMdu parigaNisalAgiruva adara BAra yA adaralilxruva darxvayxrAshiya pariNAmavAgi keLadikikxnalilx adu anuBavisuva eLeta.

\alnum{a} tUka; mananxNe paDediruva yAvudeV mApanapadadhxtiyalilx saMKAyxrUpadalilx heVLida darxvayxrAshiya motatx: \eng{what is your weight?} ninanx tUka eSuTx? \eng{goods are sold by weight not quantity} sarakugaLu tUkada parxkAra mAralapxDutatxve, rAshiya aLateyiMdalalx. 
\alnum{b} tUkada padadhxti; tUkavanunx mApanamADuva padadhxti.

\alnum{d} tUkada baTuTx; gotAtxda tUkavanunx tUgalu baLasuva loVhada bilelx \mo vu: \eng{where is the ounce weight ?} aunisxna tUkada baTuTx elilx?

\numie
\numi{4} 
\banum

\alnum{b} sanenxyu etatxbeVkAda bala, BAra.

\numi{5} 
\banum

\alnum{b} TiVke \mo vakekx koDabeVkAda bele; pArxmuKayx; mahatatxvX; mwlayx.

\bentry

\pron{veVTf}

\expl{}
\bmng

\num{2} BAra, tUka -- kaTiTx jagigxsu. 
\num{3} BAravAgisu; horeyAgisu yA aDiDxpaDisu (\rUpa\ saha).

\bentry
\word[well(3)]{well} 
\pron{velf} 
\gl{\kirxvi}
\expl{(\tara\ \eng{better}, \tama\ \eng{best}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} cenAnxgi; sariyAgi; taqpitxkaravAgi; samapaRkavAgi: \eng{the work is well done} kelasa cenAnxgi Agide. 
\num{2} sariyAgi; sariyAda riVtiyalilx: \eng{well said} sariyAda mAtu; sariyAgi heVLida mAtu. \eng{you did well to tell me} niVnu nanage heVLidudx oLeLxyadAyitu. 
\num{3} saMpUNaRvAgi; kUlaMkaSavAgi; atayxMta ecacxrikeyiMda: \eng{look well to it} adanunx ecacxrikeyiMda noVDiko. 
\num{4} bahumaTiTxge; kUDida maTiTxge; bahuteVka: \eng{he is well over retiring age} avanige, bahuteVka nivaqtitxyAguva vayasusx Agide. 
\num{5} pirxVtiyiMda; vishAvxsadiMda; senxVhadiMda: \eng{treated me well} nananxnunx vishAvxsadiMda noVDikoMDaru. 
\num{6} bahushaH; nijavAgiyU; sulaBavAgi; sakAraNavAgi; viveVkadiMda; ucita riVtiyiMda: \eng{it may well be that you are right} niVnu heVLuvudu nijavAgiyU sari irabahudu. \eng{cannot very well refuse the offer} avaru koDutetxVvenunxvudanunx aSuTx sulaBavAgi nirAkarisalAgadu. 
\num{7} utAsxhadiMda; mecucxgeyiMda; parxshaMsAtamxkavAgi: \eng{speak well of} mecucxgeyiMda nuDi. \eng{the book was well reviewed} pusatxkavanunx parxshaMsAtamxkavAgi vimashiRsalAgitutx. 
\num{8} yashasivxyAgi; anukUlavAgi: \eng{it turned out well} adu aMtayxdalilx yashasivxyAyitu, anukUlavAgi mugiyitu. 
\num{9} adaqSaTxdiMda; samayoVcitavAgi; samayakekx takakxMte, beVkAdaMte: \eng{well met}! adaqSaTxdiMda BeVTiyAde, samayakekx sariyAgi sikikxde, niVnu sikidudx oLeLxyadAyitu. 
\num{10} lABakaravAgi; parxyoVjanakaravAgi: \eng{did well for themselves} tamage lABa mADikoMDaru, lABagaLisi koMDaru. 
\num{11} hAyAgi; ArAmavAgi: \eng{we live well here} nAvu ililx hAyAgidedxVve. 
\num{12} dhArALavAgi; yatheVcaCxvAgi: \eng{the job pays well} kelasa dhArALavAgi AdAya niVDutatxde. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{as well} 
\banum
\alnum{a} jatege; saha. 
\alnum{b} anucitavalalxda; sariyAda: \eng{we may as well go} (--ra badalu) nAvu hoVgaleVbahudu. 
\alnum{c} ucita; oLeLxyadu: \eng{it would be as well to acquire} hAge koLuLxvudu ucita. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{as well as} jatege; saha: \eng{he gave me clothes as well as food} avanu nanage baTeTxya jatege AhAravanUnx koTaTx. 
\num{3} \eng{come off well} meVlemx paDe; jayashAliyAgu; kiVtiRgaLisu. 
\num{4} \eng{just as well} paravAgilalx; ciMte mADabeVkAgilalx; viSAda paDabeVkAgilalx. 
\numi{5} \eng{well and truly} 
\banum
\alnum{a} nisasxMdeVhavAgi; nijavAgi. 
\alnum{b} pUtiRyAgi; saMpUNaRvAgi. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{well aware} cenAnxgi aritu, tiLidu: \eng{well aware of the danger} apAyavanunx cenAnxgi aritiru. 
\numi{7} \eng{well away} 
\banum
\alnum{a} sAkaSuTx -- muMduvaredu, parxgati sAdhisi. 
\alnum{b} (\AmA) gADhaniderxyalilx yA pUtiR pAnamatatxnAgi. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} \eng{well begun is half done} cenAnxgi pArxraMBisida kelasa, adhaR mugiyiteMdeV lekakx; sariyAgi pArxraMBisidare adhaR mugisidaMte, sAdhisidaMteyeV. 
\num{9} \eng{well done}! (\engit{or} \eng{well run}!) (parxshaMseya mAtu) shABAsf! Bale, Bale! 
\num{10} \eng{well out of it} (\engit{or} \eng{well rid of them}) (adaqSaTxvashAtf) hAniyilalxde, naSaTxvilalxde, toMdareyilalxde -- pArAgu: \eng{you are well out of it} sadayx, adaqSaTxvashAtf adariMda pArAdeyalAlx! 
\num{11} \eng{well with (person)} (obabxna) parxshaMse, mecucxge paDe. 
\num{12} \eng{wish (person) well} (vayxkitxge) shuBa koVru; jayavAgali enunx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[well(4)]{well} 
\pron{velf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{(\sA\ \Agu) (\tara\ \eng{better}, \tama\ \eng{best}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} AroVgayxda; keSxVmada: \eng{is she well or ill?} avaLu AroVgayxvAgiruvaLoV ilalxvoV? 
\num{2} taqpitxkara; utatxma: \eng{all is well} elalxvU utatxma sithxtiyalilxve. 
\num{3} AroVgayxkaravAda: \eng{a well man} AroVgayxvaMta. 
\num{4} sUkatxvAda; yukatx; ucitavAda: \eng{it would be well to enquire} vicArisuvudu sUkatx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{all(2) nuga(4)}{$^2$all} \eng{very well.} 
\num{2} \eng{let} (\engit{or} \eng{leave) well alone} anagatayxvAgi adara taMTege hoVgabAradu; adaraSaTxkekx adirali. 
\num{3} \eng{well and good} (niNaRya \mo vanunx opipxkoLuLxvalilx) Agabahudu; sariye! \eng{if you choose to take my advice, well and good} niVnu nananx mAtu keVLuvudAdare, sariye!. 
\num{4} \eng{well enough} sAkaSuTx cenAnxgi, AkaSaRkavAgi. 
\num{5} \eng{well off} anukUla sithxtiya; sithxtivaMta; bahuteVka haNavaMtanAda. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[well(5)]{well} 
\pron{velf} 
\gl{\BAavayx}
\expl{}
\bmng
(AshacxyaR, hatAshe, otAtxya, \mo vanunx sUcisuva yA mAtanADutitxruvAga savxlapx nililxsi taruvAya matetx adanunx muMduvaresuva samayadalilx heVLuva) sari, oLeLxyadu, \mo\ mAtu. 
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{ah well} (hatAsha sithxtiyalilx) sari, biDi, inenxVnu tAneV sAdhayx? 
\num{2} \eng{oh well, it can't be helped} (gatayxMtaravilalxda sithxtiyalilx) sari, adanunx biTuTx beVre gatiyeV ilalx! 
\num{3} \eng{well, but what about Jones?} (tAtAkxlikavAgi oMdu mAtanunx opipxkoMDu) adeVnoV irabahudu. Adare joVnfsxna viSaya Enu? 
\num{4} \eng{well, here we are at last} (samAdhAna sUcisuvalilx) abAbx! konegU baMdu seVridevalAlx! 
\num{5} \eng{well, then} (EnanonxV niriVkiSxsuvalilx) muMde? AmeVle? 
\num{6} \eng{well, well}! AshacxyaR sUcisuvalilx, arareV; ela elA! 
\num{7} \eng{well, who was it?} (mAtanunx muMduvarisuvalilx) adu sari, adu yAru? 
\num{8} \eng{well, who would have thought of it?} (atayxMta AshacxyaR sUcisuvalilx) are! adu yArige tAneV gotitxtutx? 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\pron{velfrisiVvfDx} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng

\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{well-rounded} 
\pron{velfrwMDiDf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} sAMgavAda; savARMgapUNaRvAda; susaMgatavAda; cenAnxgi beLedu samaMjasavAda racaneyiMda kUDida. 
\num{2} (vAkayx, padagucaCx, \mo vugaLa \vi) suracitavAda; pariSakxqqtavAda; cenAnxgi racitavAgi susapxSATxthaRvuLaLx. 
\num{3} veYvidhayxpUNaRvAda: \eng{a well-rounded curriculum} veYvidhayxpUNaR paThayxkarxma. 
\num{4} daSaTxpuSaTx; cenAnxgi beLeda. 
\numi{5} (vayxkitxya \vi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} tuMbikoMDiruva; duMDuduMDAda meYkaTiTxna. 
\alnum{b} veYvidhayxpUNaR sAmathaRyx, shakitx, \mo vugaLiMda kUDida. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\num{2} (kirxkeTf dAMDugArana \vi) BadarxvAgi nelasida, taLavUrida; elAlx riVtiya bwliMgf anUnx edurisabalalx; sulaBavAgi auTAgada.

\numi{2} (\sA\ \eng{the West}) pAshAcxtayx: 
\banum
\alnum{a} pwvARtayx nAgarikatege vidaqshavAda yUroVpiyanf nAgarikate. 
\alnum{b} yUroVpina matutx \kanu\ amerikada kamuyxniseTxVtara rASaTxrXgaLu. 
\alnum{c} roVmanf cakArxdhipatayxda pashicxma BAga. 
\alnum{d} oMdu deVsha, nagara, \mo vugaLa pashicxma BAga. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (birxDfjx isipxVTATa) `vesfTx' eMdu kareyalAda sAdhxnadalilx kuLitukoLuLxva ATagAra. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{Far West} dUra pAshAcxtayx; (\ame) gerxVTf pelxVnfsxgaLa Acina parxdeVsha. \eng{Middle West} madhayxpAshAcxtayx; utatxra misisipige seVridaMtiruva amerikada parxdeVsha. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\expl{}
\bmng

\emng

\bentry
\word[wet(1)]{wet} 
\pron{veTf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{(\tara\ \eng{wetter}, \tama\ \eng{wettest}). }
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (niVrinalilx yA beVre darxvadalilx) toyadx; nenasida; neneda; toyisida; odedxyAda; teVvavAda; AdarxR; sikatx: \eng{wet sponge} toyadx sapxMju. 
\num{2} niVrina jate seVvisatakakx yA niVranunx baLasikoLuLxva. 
\num{3} (havA \mo vugaLa \vi) maLeya: \eng{a wet day} maLe (biVLutitxruva) dina. 
\num{4} (\ashi) (deVsha, kAnUnu, \mo vugaLa \vi) madayxda mukatx mArATakekx avakAsha -- koDuva, iruva. 
\num{5} (shAyi, baNaNx, \mo vu) AgatAne toDediruva, hacicxruva; inUnx hasiyAgiruva, sariyAgi oNagadiruva. 
\num{6} (\ashi) tapApxgi BAvisida; aviveVkada; anucita; asamaMjasa. 
\num{7} niVrina jote baLasuva: \eng{wet shampoo} niVrina jote baLasuva SAMpU. 
\num{8} (\birx) (\rAshA) (ToVri pakaSxda balaviBAgadavara daqSiTxyalilx) parxgatipara yA udAra parxvaqtitxya ToVri yA saMparxdAya vAdiya. 
\num{9} (eLemaguvina \vi) malamUtarxgaLanunx taDedukoLaLxlAgada; ucecx hoyudxkoLuLxva: \eng{is still wet at night} rAtirx hotutx inUnx ucecx hoyudxkoLuLxtatxde. 
\num{10} (\birx) (\AmA) dubaRla; meduga. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\bentry
\word[what(1)]{what} 
\pron{vATf} 
\gl{parxshAnxthaRka \gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} yAva; eMtha; eSuTx; Enu: 
\banum
\alnum{a} (anidiRSaTx saMKeyxyiMda AyuvAga \eng{what} padavU, nidiRSaTx saMKeyxyiMda AyuvAga \eng{which} padavU baLakeyalilxde): \eng{what books have you read?} niVnu yAva pusatxkagaLanunx OdididxVye? \eng{don't know what plan he will try} avanu yAva upAya baLasutAtxnoV tiLiyadu. 
\alnum{b} (\AmA) = \hyperlink{which(1)}{which}: \eng{what book have you chosen} niVnu yAva pusatxka ArisididxVye? 
\alnum{c} (vasutxgaLa motatx, saMKeyx, vivaraNe beVkeMdukoLuLxvalilx): \eng{what men, abilities, has he?} avana baLi eMtha janaru, yAva yoVgayxte -- sAmathaRyxgaLu, ive? 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (AshacxyaRsUcaka \gu) eSuTx; eMtha (mahatatx vxdudx, vicitarxvAdadudx yA asAdhAraNavAdadudx enunxvalilx): \eng{what a fool you are?} niVnu eMtha aviveVki? \eng{what impudence} eMtha, eSuTx -- dhASaTxRyx? \eng{what partial judges we are?} nAveMthA pakaSxpAtadaqSiTxya nAyxyAdhiVsharu? 
\hypertarget{what(1)3}{} 
\num{3} (saMbaMdhasUcaka \gu) yAva; eMtha; eSuTx: \eng{lend me what money you can} ninageSuTx sAdhayxvoV aSuTx haNa nanage sAla koTiTxru. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{what good} \engit{or} \eng{use is it} adariMda yAva parxyoVjana, yAva oLitu? 
\num{2} \eng{what matter?} adariMda EnAgabeVku? (`EnAdarU ciMteyilalx' eMbathaRdalilx). 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[what(2)]{what} 
\pron{vATf} 
\gl{\sanA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (parxshAnxthaRka savaRnAmavAgi) Enu; eSuTx; yAva: \eng{what is your name?} ninanx hesareVnu? \eng{don't know what she said} avaLu Enu heVLidaLoV tiLiyadu. 
\num{2} (parxshenxgaLu niSeVdhAthaRka heVLikegaLa rUpadalilx): \eng{what is the use of trying?} parxyatinxsi tAneV Enu parxyoVjana? 
\num{3} (kelavomemx inonxbabxna mAtu sariyAgi keVLisade, athaRvAgade, iruvAga, matotxmemx parxshenx, sapxSaTxne, keVLuvalilx): \eng{what? you did what?} Enu? niVnu Enu mADide aMta heVLide? \eng{what, do you really mean it?} EnaMde? nijavAgi, adu ninanx iMgitaveV? (\AmA) \eng{nice day, what?} sogasAda dina! EnaMtiVye? 
\num{4} (AshacxyaRsUcaka \sanA): eSoTxMdu!: \eng{what he must have suffered} avanu eSoTxMdu (saMkaTa) anuBavisirabeVku! 
\hypertarget{what(2)5}{} 
\hypertarget{what2 pagu5}{} 
\num{5} (saMbaMdhasUcaka \sanA) (yAvudoV) adu yA avu: \eng{what followed was unpleasant} muMdeVnAyiteMbaudu bahaLa ahitakaravAgitutx. \eng{what I have written I have written} nAnu Enu baredidedxVnoV, baredidedxVne, aSeTx. \eng{it is the poor what gets the blame} (\ashi) keTaTx hesaru baruvudu baDavarige mAtarx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{come what may} EneV barali; baMdadudx barali. 
\num{2} \eng{I know} (\engit{or} \eng{you know what he is} \engit{or} \eng{what it is)} adeVnu (yA avanu eMthavanu) eMbaudu nanage yA ninage gotutx. 
\num{3} \hyperref{kandict_k.pdf}{K}{know(1) nuga(28)}{$^1$know} \eng{what's what.} 
\num{4} \engit{or} \eng{what} heVge; athavA inenxVnu (beVre Enu?): \eng{are you trying to kill me, or what?} niVnu nananxnunx kolalxleLesutitxdidxVyoV, heVge? 
\numi{5} \eng{so what?} 
\banum
\alnum{a} AdareVnaMte?: \eng{he hates me; so what?} avanu nananxnunx devxVSisutAtxne; AdareVnaMte? adu sadayxkekx parxsakatxvalalx. 
\alnum{b} adakekx parihAravilalx, beVre upAyavilalx, mAgaRvilalx. \eng{tell you what} (\engit{or} \eng{I will tell you what)} nAnu heVLetxVne keVLu .... (nananx mAtu keVLililx). 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{what then?} muMdeVnAgabahudu (idariMda muMdeVnu pariNAmavAgabahudu?) 
\num{7} \eng{what about?} EkAgabAradu? Enu samAcAra? idakekx EnaMtiVye? ninanx aBipArxyaveVnu? nAnu heVLuvudu EneMdare.... : \eng{what about a game of chess} Iga oMdu ATa caduraMga Eke ADabAradu? \eng{what-d' you} (\engit{or} \eng{what d'ye)-call-it (etc.)} (\engit{or} \eng{what's-its}) (\engit{or} \eng{his)-name} (\engit{or} \eng{is it, what you may call it)} adeVnoV adara hesaru EnoV heVLAtxralAlx ... Acnx adeV ... adara hesaru ... EnoV aMdare ... itAyxdi. 
\num{8} \eng{what do you say} (\ame\ \eng{what say)} (\AmA) nananx salahe EneMdare ... : \eng{what do you say we have a rest} nananx salahe EneMdare nAvu vishArxMti paDeyoVNa. 
\num{9} \eng{what will people say?} jana EnaMdukoMDAru! (`idu gwravAhaRvalalx' eMbathaRdalilx). 
\num{10} \eng{what for?} Eke? EtakAkxgi? EtakokxVsakxra? 
\num{11} \eng{what have you} ninanx baLi (aMthadeV inUnx) EneVnide ... EnelAlx ive ... 
\num{12} \eng{what ho}! (dUradiMda yAranAnxdarU kUgi kareyuva udAgxradalilx yA saMdhisidAga heVLuva mAtu): `Oyf ... yAralilx?' `yArididxVri, alilx?' EnirxV. 
\num{13} \eng{what if} `AdareVnaMte?' 
\num{14} \eng{what is he?} avana vaqtitx Enu? avanu yAva kelasadalilx (nwkariyalilx) idAdxne? avana aMtasetxVnu? avanu eMthavanu? (itAyxdi). 
\num{15} \eng{what is it like?} adu heVgide (adara savxrUpa Enu?) 
\num{16} \eng{what is more} (jotege visheVSavAgi EnanAnxdarU seVrisi heVLuvAga): aSuTx mAtarxvalalx, mAtarxvalalxde. 
\num{17} \eng{what next?} (idakikxMta hecucx aviveVkavAdudu, dhASaRTxyXvAdudu yA vilakaSxNavAdudu yA hosadAdudu Enide? eMbathaRdalilx) muMdeVnu? hAgAdare -- AmeVle, muMde? 
\num{18} \eng{what not} (aneVka vasutx \mo vanunx paTiTx mADi heVLuvAga) `inUnx iMtha hatutx halavu'; inUnx EneVnoV: \eng{sheets, napkins and what not} hodeyuva magagxluhAsigegaLu, keYcwkagaLu inUnx EneVnoV. 
\num{19} \eng{what of} (adara/avana/avara/kurita) sudidx Enu, samAcAraveVnu? 
\num{20} \eng{what of it?} = \hyperlink{what2 pagu5}{?pagu? \((5)\)}. 
\num{21} \eng{what} \hyperref{kandict_t.pdf}{T}{though(1) pagu(2)}{$^1$though}. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[wheel(1)]{wheel} 
\pron{viVlf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} cakarx; gAli; rATe; rATaNa; tiguri. 
\num{2} (\kanmu\ cakarx, gAli, rATeyanunx muKayxvAda BAgavAguLaLx) yaMtarx \mo vu. 
\num{3} cakarx \mo vugaLanunx hoVluva vasutx: \eng{Catherine wheel, potter's wheel, steering wheel.} 
\num{4} (\bava dalilx) (\ashi) kAru. 
\num{5} (\ame) beYsikalf. 
\num{6} (giVte, padayx, \mo vugaLa) cikakx, mukAtxya sAlugaLu; palalxvi; caraNa. 
\num{7} BAgayxcakarx; adaqSaTxda EriLitagaLu: \eng{wheel of Fortune} BAgayxcakarx. 
\num{8} (\sA\ seYnikavUyxha calaneyalilx) cakarxcalane; daMDavaqtatx calane; oMdu koneyalilx kiVlisiruva reVKe, A kiVlina meVle tiruguvAga AguvaMtha calane. 
\num{9} (\ame) (\ashi) doDaDx manuSayx; gaNayxvayxkitx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{at the wheel} 
\banum
\alnum{a} cakarx hiDidu; vAhana naDesutAtx yA haDagina calane nideRVshisutAtx. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (vayxvahAra, vidayxmAna, \mo vanunx) hatoVTiyalilxDutAtx; niyaMtirxsutAtx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{break a} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{butterfly nuga}{butterfly} \eng{on the wheel.} 
\num{3} \eng{break on the wheel} (shikiSxsabeVkAdavaranunx madhayxyugadalilx mADutitxdadx hAge) daMDana cakarxkekx kaTiTx citarxhiMse mADu, kolulx. 
\num{4} \eng{go on} (\engit{or} \eng{oiled) wheels} sulalitavAgi hoVgu, calisu. 
\num{5} \hyperref{kandict_o.pdf}{O}{oil(2) pagu(3)}{$^2$oil} \eng{the wheels.} 
\num{6} \eng{put a} \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{spoke(1) pagu}{$^1$spoke} \eng{in (person's) wheel.} 
\num{7} \eng{right wheel} (\engit{or} \eng{left wheel)} (kavAyitinalilx AjAcnxshabadxvAgi) balakekx (yA eDakekx) daMDavaqtatxvAgi tirugi. 
\numi{8} \eng{wheel of life} 
\banum
\alnum{a} = \hyperref{kandict_z.pdf}{Z}{zoetrope}{zoetrope}. 
\alnum{b} (bwdadhxdhamaRdalilx heVLuva) (vayxkitxya) janamxcakarx; niraMtara janAmxMtara cakarxgaLu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{9} \eng{wheels of life} jiVvAdhAra vAyxpAragaLu; jiVvanacakarxgaLu. 
\hypertarget{wheel(1) pagu(10)}{} 
\numi{10} \eng{wheels within wheels} 
\banum
\alnum{a} sUkaSxmX jaTila yaMtarx. 
\alnum{b} (\AmA) taMtarx doLagina taMtarx; gupatx taMtarx paraMpare; hutatxdalilx hutatx. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\num{4} (kAlada \vi) eSuTx hiMde?

\num{6} (saMbaMdhasUcaka \kirxvi) (kAlakekx saMbaMdhisidaMte) Aga: \eng{the time when such things could happen is past} aMtha GaTanegaLu naDeyuva kAla mugiduhoVgide. \eng{there are occasions when one must yield} kelavomemx nAvu soVlabeVkAgutatxde. \eng{there are times when I would cry} nAnu aLuva yA aLabeVku enisuva samayagaLu kelavive.

hotutx; tAriVKu; dina; saMdaBaR: \eng{he told me the when and the how of it} avanu adu naDeda dina, naDeda riVti -- elalxvanUnx heVLida. \eng{fixed the when and where} yAvAga, elilx enunxvudanunx nidhaRrisida. 
\emng
\eentry

\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} elilx? etatx? yAva kaDe? yAva -- dikikxnalilx, dikikxnatatx, kaDeyalilx?: \eng{where does the argument lead?} vAda yAva dikikxnalilx sAgide? \eng{where does it concern us?} adu namage elilx saMbaMdhapaDutatxde? 
\numi{3} 
\banum

\num{5} (saMbaMdhasUcaka \kirxvi vAgi)(sathxLa \mo vugaLa hiMde baMdAga) elilx yA elilxge: \eng{places where they meet} avaru BeVTi mADuva sathxLagaLalilx.

\bentry
\word[while(1)]{while} 
\pron{veYlf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (kelasa \mo vakekx hiDida, viniyoVgisida, kaLeda) hotutx; veVLe; samaya; avadhi; kAla: \eng{go away for a while} savxlapx hotutx horaTuhoVgu. 
\numi{2} 
\banum
\alnum{a} beVroMdu kirxyeya, kelasada madheyx, naDuve. 
\alnum{b} (\kAparx) Aga; A hotutx; A samayada -- madheyx, naDuve. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} savxlapx kAla, samaya: \eng{have not seen you a while} savxlapxkAladiMda ninanxnunx noVDilalx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{a good} (\engit{or} \eng{great) while} bahaLa kAla; sumAru hotutx. 
\num{2} \eng{all the while} A iDiV samayadalilx; udadxkUkx. 
\num{3} \eng{between whiles} (beVre, itara kelasagaLu, GaTanegaLu, \mo vugaLa) naDuve. 
\num{4} \eng{for a long while} bahaLa kAladiMda: \eng{have not seen him for a long while} bahaLa kAladiMdalU avananunx noVDilalx. 
\num{5} \eng{(for) a while} savxlapx kAladiMda. 
\num{6} \eng{in a} (\engit{or} \eng{little) while} beVgane; koMca, savxlapx -- hotitxnalilx. 
\num{7} \eng{once in a while} AgaloV IgaloV omemx; yAvAgalAdaromemx. \eng{he will make it worth your while} ninage takakxSuTx parxtiPala koDutAtxne. 
\numi{8} \eng{the while} (\engit{or} \eng{whilst)} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\kAparx) Aga; A hotutx; A veVLe. 
\alnum{b} beVre kelasada samayadalilx. 
\hypertarget{while(1) pagu(9)}{} 
\eanum
\numie
\num{9} \eng{worth one's while} parxyoVjanakAriyAda; upayukatx; sAthaRka: \eng{it isn't worth while going there} alilxge hoVguvudariMda EnU parxyoVjanavilalx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[whip(1)]{whip} 
\pron{vipf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{(\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{whipped}; \vakaq\ \eng{whipping}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} taTakakxne, Pakakxne -- calisu, tegeduko, kiVLu, hiri, kasiduko, hoDe, nugugx, horaDu (\akirx\ saha): \eng{whip out a sword} sarakakxne katitx hiri. \eng{whip away the tablecloth} meVjina musukanunx pakakxne eLedu hAku. \eng{whip off your coat} taTakakxne ninanx koVTanunx kaLacu, kitetxse. 
\num{2} (huri, koVlu, \mo vakekx) hatatxnAgi dAra sututx. 
\num{3} cAvaTiyiMda -- hoDe, bArisu, tiVDu. 
\num{4} cAvaTiyiMda hoDedu -- naDesu, ODisu, oTuTx seVrisu. 
\num{5} balavAgi dUSisu, tegaLu. 
\num{6} (moTeTx, hAlina kene, \mo vanunx) (noregaTuTxvaMte) goTAyisu; kaDe; tiVDu. 
\num{7} (\birx) (\ashi) kadi; lapaTAyisu: \eng{who has whipped my pen?} yAru nananx penanxnunx kadadxvaru? 
\numi{8} (\ashi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} miVru; miVrisu. 
\alnum{b} soVlisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{whip in} (beVTenAyigaLanunx) (cAvaTiyiMda) oTuTxgUDisu, oTiTxge seVrisu. 
\num{2} \eng{whip off} = \hyperlink{whip(1)}{$^1$whip\((1)\)}. 
\num{3} \eng{whip on} kelasakekx toDagisu; kAyaRkekx perxVrisu. 
\numi{4} \eng{whip up} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (BAvane \mo vanunx) keraLisu; parxcoVdisu. 
\alnum{b} (hAjarAgalu) kare niVDu; AdeVshisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[whip(2)]{whip} 
\pron{vipf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} cAvaTi; cabauku; koraDa; caDi; cabaka; cATi; kashe; bArukoVlu. 
\num{2} beVTegArana sahAyaka; beVTenAyigaLu cedaradaMte maMde hoDeyuva, beVTe sahAyaka. 
\numi{3} (shAsanasaBe \mo vugaLalilx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} shisutxpAlaka; pAliRmeMTinalilx oMdu pakaSxda sadasayxra shisutx noVDikoLuLxvudu, avaru saBegaLige baruvaMte noVDikoLuLxvudu, avarige beVkAda tiLivaLikeyanunx koDuvudu, \mo\ kAyaRkAkxgi neVmitanAdavanu. 
\alnum{b} (\birx) shisutx nirUpa; hAjarAti hukumu; shisutxpAlakanu sadasayxrige hAjarAguvaMte kaLuhisida karepatarx: \eng{three-line whip} mUrusAlina ni\rUpa\ 
\alnum{c} pakaSxda shisutx matutx AdeVshagaLu: \eng{asked for the Labour whip} leVbarf pakaSxda AdeVshagaLanunx koVridaru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} gADiya cAlaka; baMDi hoDeyuvavanu: \eng{he is a good whip} avanu cenAnxgi gADi hoDeyutAtxne. 
\num{5} kapipx matutx hagagxda etutxyaMtarx. 
\num{6} (kaDeda kene, beNeNx, \mo vugaLiMda tayArisida) oMdu (sihi) BakaSxyX. 
\num{7} kene, moTeTxgaLu, \mo vanunx norebaruvaMte kaDeyuvike, goTAyisuvike. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\eng{fair} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{crac(1) nuga(3)}{$^1$crack} \eng{of the whip.} 
\emng
\eentry

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} siLuLx -- hAku, hoDe; siVTi Udu; shiLeLx hAku. 
\num{2} (saMkeVta niVDalu yA AshacxyaR yA tirasAkxra sUcisalu) siLeLx hAku; siLeLx hAki -- saMkeVta koDu, AshacxyaR yA tirasAkxra sUcisu. 
\num{3} (hakikx) siLiLxna shabadxmADu. 
\num{4} (kiSxpaNi, gALi, \mo vu) siLuLxsadidxnoDane royayxne calisu. 
\num{5} (nAyi \mo vanunx) kareyalu siLuLxhAku. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{let (person) go whistle} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (obabxna Ase, apeVkeSxgaLanunx) upeVkiSxsu; kaDegaNisu; lekikxsadiru: \eng{he said we could go whistle for our money} namamx haNakAkxgi siLuLx hAkutatx kUruvaMte avanu heVLida (aMdare kaDegaNisida). 
\alnum{b} (obabxna mAtu \mo vugaLa virudadhx) tirasAkxradiMda -- nagu, AshacxyaR sUcisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} \eng{whistle down the wind} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (DeVge beVTe) DeVgeyanunx (hAralu) biDu; hArihoVguvaMte biDu. 
\alnum{b} keYbiDu; tore; biTuTxbiDu; tayxjisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{whistle for} (\AmA) vayxthaRvAgi -- haMbalisu, bAyibAyi biDu; hapahapisu. 
\num{4} \eng{whistle for a wind} (nivARta sathxLadalilx sikikxkoMDa nAvikaru) gALigAgi -- siLuLxhAku, haMbalisu. 
\num{5} \eng{whistle in the dark} katatxlalilx siLeLxhAku; hedarilalxveMbaMte naTisu; Bayavanunx, BiVtiyanunx -- gelulx, jayisu. 
\num{6} \eng{whistle up} (nAyi, seVvaka, \mo vanunx) siLeLx hAki, Udi -- kare, baruvaMte heVLu. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word{who} 
\pron{hU} 
\gl{\sanA}
\expl{}
\bmng
(divxtiyA viBakitx \eng{whom} \ucAcx\ hUmf yA \AmA \eng{who} \ucAcx\ hU; SaSiThxVviBakitx \eng{whose} \ucAcx\ hUsfZ). 
\bnum
\numi{1} (parxshAnxthaRka) 
\banum
\alnum{a} yAru? yAvanu? yAvaLu?: \eng{who said so?} hAge heVLidavaru yAru? \eng{who would have thought of it?} (yArU adanunx yoVcisutitxralilalx eMba athaRdalilx) yAru tAneV adanunx yoVcisutitxdadxru? \eng{whom} \engit{or} \eng{who did you see?} niVnu yAranunx noVDide? 
\alnum{b} yAru? eMthavanu? eMthavaLu? eMthavaru?: \eng{who am I to object?} AkeSxVpisalu nAnu yAru? (nanageVnu hakukx?) 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (niSeVdhasUcaka parxshenxyAgi) \eng{who would have thought of it?} hAgeMdu yAru tAneV yoVcisidadxru? 
\num{3} A (vayxkitx); aMtha vayxkitx: \eng{any one who wishes can come} yAru baralu iciPxsutAtxroV avaru barabahudu. \eng{the woman who you met?} niVnu BeVTimADida heMgasu. \eng{the man who you saw} niVnu noVDida vayxkitx (koneya eraDu udAharaNegaLalilx \eng{whom} sariyAda parxyoVga, Adare sAmAnayx saMdaBaRgaLalilx \eng{who} eMdu parxyoVga). 
\num{4} matutx yA Adare avanu, avaLu, avaru, \mo: \eng{sent it to Ram, who gave it to Lakshman} adanunx rAmanige kaLuhisida, matutx (yA Adare) avanu adanunx lakaSxmXNanige koTaTx. 
\num{5} (\pArxparx) yAru; yAreV Agali; yAvudeV vayxkitx; yAvanu(Lu): \eng{who steals my purse steals trash} yAru nananx ` pasaR' nunx kadiyuvaroV avaru kelasakekx bAradadxnunx kadadxhAge lekakx (yArAdarU nananx haNa kadadxre nanageVnU naSaTxvilalx eMbathaRdalilx). \eng{whom the gods love die young} yAra meVle deVvara kaqpe ideyoV aMthavaru cikakx vayasisxnalelxV (beVga) sAyutAtxre. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{as who should say} hAgeMdu heVLidavana riVtiyalilx; yAroV hAge heVLidareMbaMte. 
\num{2} \eng{who-does-what dispute} \engit{or} \eng{strike} (jagaLa, vivAda, saMpu, \mo vugaLa \vi) yAru yAvudanunx mADabeVku enunxvudu; yAra kelasa Enu enunxvudu. 
\num{3} \eng{who goes there?} = \hyperref{kandict_g.pdf}{G}{gopagu67}{go} (\pagu\ \eng{67}). 
\num{4} \eng{who is it} (hesaru nenapAgadiruvAga) adu yAroV obabxru. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[wild(1)]{wild} 
\pron{veYlfDx} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (pArxNi yA sasayxda \vi) vanayx; kADu; sAkirada yA kaqSimADi beLasilalxda; nisagaRda sahaja sithxtiyalilxruva: \eng{wild plant} kADu giDa. \eng{wild duck} kADu bAtu. 
\num{2} rUkaSx; asaMsakxqqta; anAgarika; oraTu; nayavalalxda: \eng{wild Indians} anAgarika (reDf) iMDiyanf janaru 
\num{3} (daqshayx, sathxLa, \mo vugaLa \vi) kADu; pALu; hALu (suriyuva); hALubidadx; nijaRnavAda; baMjaru: \eng{this is still wild country} idu inUnx pALAgi uLidiruva parxdeVsha. 
\num{4} (kudure, beVTe hakikx, \mo vugaLa \vi) bedaruva; hedari ODuva; hatitxra hoVgagoDada. 
\num{5} kaTuTxniTiTxlalxda; hatoVTi miVrida; laMgulagAmilalxda; savxcaCxMdavaqtitxya; ucACxqqMKala; avayxvasethxya; saMparxdAya shiSATxcAragaLanunx lekikxsada: \eng{a wild fellow} savxcaCxMdavaqtitxya manuSayx. 
\num{6} (isipxVTu eleya \vi) ATagAraneV nidhaRrisuva beleyanunx hoMdida. 
\num{7} ugarx; BayaMkara; parxcaMDa; GoVra: \eng{a wild wind} parxcaMDa birugALi. 
\num{8} tiVvorxVtAsxhada; AveVshada; uderxVkada; hucecxdadx; unamxtatx: \eng{wild with excitement} saMBarxmadiMda hucAcxgi. 
\num{9} (muKaBAva, cahare, \mo vugaLa \vi) mativikala; vayxgarx; parxkuSxbadhx; citatxBarxmaNe yA baudidhxvikalapxda;unAmxdada lakaSxNagaLu toVruva. 
\num{10} (\AmA) siTiTxgedadx; ugarxroVSada; BayaMkaravAgi koVpagoMDa: \eng{makes me wild} nanage roVSa tarutatxde. \eng{a wild rage} ugarxroVSa. 
\num{11} avicArita; Aturada; duDukina; gotutxguriyilalxda; sikAkxbaTeTxya; sariyAgi AloVcane mADada: \eng{a wild guess} duDukina Uhe. \eng{a wild shot} sikAkxbaTeTx hoDeda guMDina hoDeta. \eng{a wild venture} gotutxguriyilalxda sAhasa. 
\num{12} (\AmA) (yAvudeV oMdara \vi) tiVvArxnurakatx; kaTATxBimAniyAda; kaDuniSeThxya; tiVvorxVtAsxhadiMda kUDida; hucucxhiDida: \eng{wild about the new scheme} hosa yoVjaneya hucucx hiDida. 
\num{13} saMBarxmada; AnaMdakaravAda. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{run wild} 
\banum
\alnum{a} hucAcxbaTeTx beLe yA aledADu. 
\alnum{b} shisutx, aMke, niyaMtarxNagaLilalxdiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{wild and woolly} oraTAda; nayavilalxda; rUkaSx. 
\num{3} \eng{sow one's wild} \hyperref{kandict_o.pdf}{O}{oat pagu(3)}{oats}. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
%\hyperdef{W}{will(1)}{}\word[will(1)]{will} 
\pron{vilf}
sahAyaka
\gl{\kirx}
\bmng
(utatxmapuruSa, madhayxma puruSa, taqtiVya puruSa, \Eva\ vataRmAna \eng{will}; madhayxma puruSa, \Eva\ vataRmAna pArxparx. \eng{wilt} \ucAcx\ vilfTx; \BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{would} \ucAcx\ vuDf). (heVLike, Ajecnx yA parxshenxgaLalilx) BaviSayxkAla sUcaka: \eng{you will regret this} niVnidakekx viSAdapaDutitxVye. \eng{you will leave at once} niVnu kUDaleV horaTuhoVga beVku. \eng{will you come} niVnu barutitxVyA? 
\bnum
\num{1} bayasu; Ashisu; udedxVshisu; iciPxsu: (\pArxparx) \eng{what wilt thou?} ninage Enu beVku? \eng{what would they?} avaru Enu iciCxsuvaru? 
\num{2} (iceCx, opipxge yA olavugaLanunx) sUcisu; Ashisu; AsepaDu; beVkAgu: \eng{come when you will} ninage yAvAga beVkoV, Aga bA. 
\num{3} opupx; samamxtisu: \eng{would not go any further} (idakikxMta inUnx) hecucx muMduvariyalu opepxnu. 
\num{4} rUDhiya, aBAyxsa yA anivAyaR parxvaqtitxyanunx sUcisu: \eng{will sit there for hours} gaMTegaTaTxle alilx kuLitukoLuLxtAtxne. \eng{accidents will happen} apaGAtagaLu saMBavisutatxve, AgiyeV Agutatxve, naDadeV naDeyutatxve. 
\num{5} (utatxmapuruSadalilx) (nidhARra, udedxVsha, iceCx, \mo vanunx) sUcisu: \eng{I will not be caught again} nAnu matetx sikikxbiVLuvudilalx. \eng{I will return soon} nAnu beVga vApasAgutetxVne. 
\num{6} shakitx, sAmathaRyx sUcisu: \eng{the jar will hold a kilo} jADi oMdu kiloV hiDisutatxde. \eng{I will manage it} nAnu adanunx nivaRhisabalelx (nivaRhisutetxVne). 
\num{7} saMBava yA niriVkeSxyanunx sUcisu: \eng{that will be my wife} avaLu nananx heMDati AgutAtxLe (Aguva saMBavavide). 
\num{8} (\AmA) = \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{shall(5)}{shall(5)}: \eng{I would like to disagree} nAnu opapxliciPxsuvudilalx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{I wouldn't know} (niriVkiSxsuva hAge) nanage tiLiyadu; nanage gotitxlalx. 
\numi{2} \eng{will do} (\AmA) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (koVrikeyanunx neraveVrisuva mAtAgi) Agali; hAge mADutetxVne. \eng{we would have come if you had told us} niVnu modaleV heVLidadxre nAvu barutitxdedxvu. 
\alnum{b} \eng{that will} \hyperref{kandict_d.pdf}{D}{do(1) nuga(34)}{$^1$do} (\pagu\ \eng{34}). 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{would God} deVvaru mADisidadxre, karuNisidadxre: \eng{would God that I were dead} nAnu sAyuvaMte deVvaru anugarxhisidadxre cenAnxgitutx! 
\num{4} \eng{would I were} iceCxpaDuve; Ashisuve: \eng{would I were a bird} nAnoMdu hakikxyAgidadxre (cenAnxgitutx).

\bentry
\word[will(2)]{will} 
\pron{vilf} 
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum

\bmng
\bnum

\alnum{b} (nidiRSaTx dikikxniMda biVLuva yA visheVSa riVtiya) gALi; mAruta: \eng{north wind} utatxra mAruta; baDagu gALi. \eng{fair wind} (haDagina calanege) anukUlavAda gALi. \eng{contrary wind} parxtikUla mAruta; edurugALi. \eng{constant wind} oMdu sathxLadalilx yAvAgalU oMdeV dikikxnalilx biVsuva gALi; gotutxgALi; niyata mAruta.

\bentry
\word{window} 
\pron{viMDoV} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} kiTaki; beLaku, gALi -- kaMDi; gavAkiSx; vAtAyana; jananxlu. 
\num{2} kiTakiya gAju: \eng{broke the windmill} kiTakiya gAjanunx oDeda. 
\num{3} gamanaviTuTx, lakaSxyXviTuTx noVDuva yA kalitukoLuLxva -- avakAsha: \eng{English language is a windmill on the world} iMgilxSf BASe parxpaMcavanunx viVkiSxsalu anukUlavAguva oMdu kiTaki. 
\numi{4} kiTaki: 
\banum
\alnum{a} aMgaDiya muMBAgada kiTakiya hiMde sAmAnugaLanunx aMdavAgi joVDisiDuva jAga, sathxLa. 
\alnum{b} bAyxMkinalilx haNa, raMgamaMdira, \mo vugaLalilx TikeTuTx \mo vanunx koDuva goVDeyalilxna kaMDi. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{5} (lakoVTeya meVlina) terapu; kiTaki; oLage bareda viLAsa kANuvaMte madheyx pAradashaRka kAgada mucicxda lakoVTeya terapu. 
\num{6} (aMtarikaSx nwkeya nidiRSaTx yAnakekx anukUlavAguva havAmAnada yA KAgoVLika garxhagatiya parisithxtigaLalilx parxshasatxvAgiruva) kAlAvadhi; kAlAvakAsha. 
\num{7} rADArfniMda patetxyAgadaMte taDe oDuDxva, aMtarikaSxdalilx teVlibiTaTx, teLaLxneya loVhapaTeTxgaLu. 
\numi{8} gavAkaSx: 
\banum
\alnum{a} datAtxMshagaLa nidiRSaTx BAgavu viVkaSxkarige kANuvaMte daqshayx parxkAshana GaTaka \eng{(VDU)} oMdaralilx Ayadx BAga. 
\alnum{b} viduyxtAkxMta taraMgagaLa peYki yAva BAgakekx nidiRSaTx mAdhayxmavu pArakavAgiruvudoV A BAga. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{9} (kirxyege, caTuvaTikege) anukUlavAguva kAlAvadhi yA kAlAvakAsha. 
\num{10} taraMgakiTaki; mAdhayxmavoMdakekx pAradashaRkate hoMdiruva viduyxtAkxMtiVya taraMgAMtaragaLa haravu, vAyxpitx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{blank} (\engit{or} \eng{blind} \engit{or} \eng{false) windmill} husi -- kiTaki; (terapilalxda) toVkeR kiTaki. 
\num{2} \eng{have all (one's) goods in the (front} \engit{or} \eng{shop-) windmill} bAhAyxkaSaRNe hoMdiru; keVvala toVkeRge yA meVlunoVTakekx mAtarx aMdavAgiru, suMdaravAgi kANu. 
\num{3} \eng{out of the windmill} (\AmA) lekakxkekx, gamanakekx tegedukoLaLxda; parigaNanege horatAda; lekikxsada.
