\bentry 
\word{windy}
\pron{viMDi} 
\gl{\gu} 
\expl{(\tara\ \eng{windier}, \tama\ \eng{windiest}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} gALige IDAda, oDiDxda, sikikxda: \eng{windy hill top} gALigoDiDxda beTaTxda netitx. 
\num{2} birugALiya; gALi joVrAgiruva, balavAgi biVsuva: \eng{a windy night} gALi joVrAgiruva rAtirx.

\bentry

\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{3} vimAnada rekekx; rekekxyaMtha adara sahAyaka BAga.

\alnum{b} ATada meYdAnada pakakxBAga.

\num{11} (\aMrashA\ matutx \savi) yAvudeV aMgaracaneya pAshaRvxBAga, horacAcu.

\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{clip (person's) wings .} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxya) kAyaRcaTuvaTikegaLanunx kuMThitagoLisu, siVmitagoLisu. 
\alnum{b} (vayxkitxya) mahatAvxkAMkeSxgaLige taDe oDuDx. 
\alnum{c} (vayxkitxya) haNakAsina sAvxtaMtarxyXvanunx moTakugoLisu; (vayxkitxya) KacuRvecacx KoVtA mADu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{(come) on the wings of wind} vAyuveVgadalilx (bA). 
\num{3} \eng{lend} (\engit{or} \eng{give) wings to} vayxkitxyanunx yA vasutxvanunx tavxregoLisu, beVga AguvaMte mADu. 
\num{4} \eng{on a wing and a prayer} yashasisxna tiVrA alapx avakAsha hoMdi. 
\num{5} \eng{on the wing} hArutatx; calisutatx; parxyANadalilx. 
\hyperdef{W}{wing(1) pagu(6)}{} 
\num{6} \eng{spread} (\engit{or} \eng{stretch) one's wings} (\rUpa) saMpUNaR shakitxsAmathaRyx beLesiko; shakitxsAdhayxte garigedaruvaMte mADu. 
\num{7} \eng{sprout wings} rekekx mUDisu; shakitx moLeyisu: \eng{his wings are sprouting} avanige (deVvategaLaMte) rekekxgaLu mUDutitxve, moLeyutitxve; avanalilxruva deVvatA guNagaLu, shakitxgaLu parxkaTavAgutitxve. 
\hyperdef{W}{wing(1) pagu(8)}{}

\num{9} \eng{take wing} hArihoVgu; meVleVru. 
\num{10} \eng{waiting in the wings} (\rUpa) saMpUNaR sidadhxteyalilx; sidadhxvAgi niMtu.

\alnum{a} taMtiyAgi eLeda loVha. 
\alnum{b} (loVhada) taMti; kaMbi; sarige. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} viduyxtf (parxvAha oyuyxva) taMti. 
\num{3} (\kanmu\ \ame) (\AmA) taMti yA keVbalf sudidx; tAru; taMti samAcAra: \eng{sent me a wire} nanagoMdu taMti, tAru kaLuhisidAdxne. 
\num{4} beVlige kaTaTxlu yA viduyxdAvxhakavAgi baLasuva taMtiya udadx yA parxmANa. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{by wire} TeligArxM, taMti - mUlaka. 
\num{2} \eng{get the} (\engit{or} \eng{one's) wires crossed} (\rUpa) galibiligoLuLx; goMdalavAgu; tapupx athaR mADiko. 
\numi{3} \eng{pull (the) wires} 
\banum
\alnum{a} sUtarxda goMbe \mo vanunx ADisu. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) rahasayxvAgi parxBAva biVru; vashiVli naDesu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\num{3} sUkaSx mxviveVcaneya; vAyxvahArika jANatanada; loVkajAcnxnada; yukAtxyukatx parijAcnxnavuLaLx; sUkaSx mxgarxhikeya; tiLivaLikeyuLaLx. 
\num{4} arivu, viveVka, baudidhxvaMtike -- sUcisuva: \eng{with a wise nod of the head} arivuLaLxvanaMte taledUgi.

\num{2} \eng{came away as wise as} (\engit{or} \eng{not much wiser} \engit{or} \eng{no wiser} \engit{or} \eng{none the wiser)} hoVda puTaTx, baMda puTaTx; hoVgi baMdadedxV horatu hiMdigiMta hececxVnU tiLiyalilalx. 
\hyperdef{W}{wise(1) pagu(3)}{} 
\num{3} \eng{put a person wise (to)} (\AmA) (EnanAnxdarU) tiLisu; (oMdara bagegx) arivu mUDisu, tiLiya heVLu. 
\num{4} \eng{wise after the event} keTaTxmeVle baudidhx baMtu; oMdu GaTane naDeduhoVda meVle, saninxveVsha kaLedu hoVdameVle -- athaR mADikoLaLxbalalxvanAgi yA niBAyisabalalxvanAgi.

\num{1} bayasu; koVru; iciPxsu; apeVkiSxsu; Ashisu; hAreYsu: \eng{I wish him happy} avanu suKavAgiraleMdu hAreYsuve. 
\num{2} EnanenxV mADalu, noVDalu (itAyxdi) -- bayasu, Ashisu: \eng{they say they wish peace} tAvu shAMti bayasutetxVve enunxtAtxre avaru. 
\num{3} bayasu; hAreYsu: \eng{I wish you joy} niVnu saMtoVSavAgiraleMdu bayasutetxVne. 
\num{4} (\AmA) (obabxna meVle) horisu; AroVpisu. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word{with} 
\pron{vitf} 
\gl{\upa}
\expl{{}
\bmng
oDane; kUDa; oMdige; saMgaDa; jotege; joteyalilx; sameVta; sahita: 
\banum
\alnum{a} upakaraNadiMda; sAdhanadiMda (eMbathaRgaLalilx): \eng{cut with a knife} cAkuviniMda katatxrisu. 
\alnum{b} sahavAsadalilx; sAhacayaRdalilx; oDanATadalilx: \eng{lives with his mother} tananx tAyiyoDane vAsisutAtxne. 
\alnum{c} kAraNadiMda; deseyiMda: \eng{trembles with fear} hedarikeyiMda naDugutAtxne. \eng{in bed with fever} javxradiMda hAsige hiDididAdxne. 
\alnum{d} hoMdiruva; oLagoMDa; uLaLx: \eng{man with dark hair} kapupxkUdalina manuSayx. \eng{a vase with handles} hiDigaLuLaLx kalasha. 
\alnum{e} parisithxtiyalilx: \eng{sleep with the windows open} kiTakigaLanunx teredu malagiko. \eng{a holiday with all the expenses paid} KacuRvecacxgaLanenxlAlx Barisida rajAparxvAsa. 
\alnum{f} riVtiyalilx; anusarisida yA parxkaTisida bageyalilx: \eng{behaved with dignity} GanateyiMda naDedukoMDa. \eng{spoke with vehemence} AveVshadiMda mAtADida. \eng{handle with care} jAgarUkateyiMda muTuTx, hiDi. \eng{won with ease} sulaBavAgi gedadx. 
\alnum{g} sahamata; sAmarasayx; hoMdike; oDaMbaDike; samamxti; sahAnuBUti: \eng{sympathise with} sahAnuBUti iru, toVru. \eng{I believe with you that it is true} adu nijaveMdu nanagU ninanx hAgeyeV anisutatxde, nAnu ninanxMteyeV opupxtetxVne. \eng{blue does not go with green} niVliyU hasurU hoMduvudilalx. 
\alnum{h} asamamxti; viroVdha; sapxdheR: \eng{fight with} oDane yA virudadhx hoVrADu, kAdADu. \eng{incompatible with} oDane -- asamaMjasavAgi, asaMgatavAgi, hoMdikeyilalxde. \eng{argue with} oDane yA virudadhx vAdisu. 
\alnum{i} (yAvudoV oMdara) javAbAdxri; hoNe; vasha; suPaduR: \eng{the decision rests with you} nidhARra ninanx keYyalilxde, ninage biTaTxdudx. \eng{leave the child with me} maguvanunx nananx hatitxra, nananx vashadalilx biDu. 
\alnum{j} vasutx; padAthaR: \eng{made with gold} -- cinanxdiMda mADidudx. 
\alnum{k} seVrike; pUreYke; padAthaR, guNa, parisara, \mo vanunx hoMdiruvudu: \eng{fill it with water} adakekx niVru tuMbau, adanunx niVriniMda tuMbisu. \eng{threaten with dismissal} vajA mADuvudAgi hedarisu. \eng{decorate with garlands} hUmAlegaLiMda alaMkarisu, siMgarisu. 
\alnum{l} kuritu; saMbaMdhavAgi: \eng{be patient with them} avaroDane tALemxyiMdiru. \eng{how are things with you} niVnu heVgididxVye? ninanx sithxtigatigaLu heVgive? \eng{is it well with you?} niVnu keSxVmave? \eng{what do you want with me} naninxMda ninageVnu beVkAgide? \eng{nothing wrong with expressing one's opinions} tananx aBipArxyagaLanunx tiLisuvudaralilx yAva tapUpx ilalx. 
\alnum{m} saMbaMdhisidaMte; kAraNavanunx anusarisi; kAraNakekx anuguNavAgi: \eng{changes with the weather} havAmAnadoDane, havAmAnakekx anuguNavAgi badalAyisutatxde. \eng{keeps pace with the cost of living} jiVvanavecacxkekx anuguNavAgi, jiVvanavecacxvanunx anusarisi sAgutatxde, hejejxyiDutatxde. 
\alnum{n} AdAgUyx; hAgidadxrU; hAgideyeMdu opipxdadxrU, parigaNisidadxrU: \eng{with all your faults, we like you} ninanx doVSagaLu eSeTxV idadxrU ninanx kaMDare namage pirxVti. \eng{with all his riches, he is the simplest of men} avanalilx aSoTxMdu aishavxyaRvidadxrU, avanobabx atayxMta saraLa vayxkitx.} 
\eanum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\bentry
\word[wolf(1)]{wolf} 
\pron{vulfphx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{wolves} \ucAcx\ vulfvxsfZ). }
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} toVLa; vaqka. 
\num{2} hoTeTxbAka yA durAseya vayxkitx. 
\num{3} (\ashi) toVLa; mitimiVrida kAmuka parxvaqtitxyavanu; heMgasaranunx kADi keDisuvavanu; laMpaTa. 
\numi{4} (\saM) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (piTiVlu \mo\ kamAnu -- vAdayxgaLalilxna) kelavu savxragaLalilx baruva kakaRsha shabadx. 
\alnum{b} kelavu haLeya AgaRnf vAdayxgaLalilxna taMti miVTidAga baruva -- apashurxti, apasavxra. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{cry wolf (too often)} toVLa baMtu toVLa eMdu bobebx hAku, kUgebibxsu; apAya baMdideyeMdu suLuLx kUgebibxsi, nijavAda apAya odagidAga yArU sahAyakekx baradaMtha eDavaTuTx taMduko. 
\num{2} \eng{have} (\engit{or} \eng{hold) a wolf by the ears} hiDididadxrU kaSaTx, biTaTxrU kaSaTx eMba ikakxTiTxnalilxru. 
\num{3} \eng{keep the wolf from the door} hoTeTxgilalxde sAyuvudanunx tapipxsiko; dAridarxyx mAri maneyoLakekx hogada hAge noVDiko. 
\num{4} \eng{lone wolf} EkAMtapirxya; EkAkiyAgi jiVvisuvudakekx, kelasa mADuvudakekx hecucx iSaTxpaDuva vayxkitx. 
\num{5} \eng{throw to the wolves} dayAdAkiSxNayxvilalxde (obabx vayxkitx \mo varanunx) balikoDu. 
\num{6} \eng{wolf in sheep's clothing} goVmuKa vAyxGarx; kurimeYya toVLa; senxVha naTisuva dhUtaR. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[wonder(1)]{wonder} 
\pron{vaMDarf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} AshacxyaR; acacxri; visamxya; kwtuka; beragu; bekakxsa; coVdayx: \eng{was filled with wonder} AshacxyaRBaritanAda. \eng{looked at him in open-mouthed wonder} beraginiMda bAyi biTuTxkoMDu avananunx noVDida. 
\num{2} soVjiga; kwtuka; vicitarx yA vilakaSxNa yA aduBxta -- vayxkitx, vasutx, mAdari, GaTane, \mo vu. 
\num{3} AshacxyaRkaravAda saMgati, viSaya: \eng{it is a wonder you were not hurt} ninage hAniyAgadidudxdu AshacxyaR, oMdu AshacxyaRveV sari. 
\num{4} (visheVSaNavAgi) pavADa; soVjiga; aduBxtavAda yA atAyxshacxyaRkara guNagaLu \mo vu: \eng{a wonder drug} pavADadaMtha madudx. \eng{a wonder child} aduBxta (shakitxgaLuLaLx) magu, huDuga.} 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{do} (\engit{or} \eng{work) wonders} 
\banum
\alnum{a} pavADagaLanunx mADu; aduBxta kAyaRgaLanunx sAdhisu. 
\alnum{b} aduBxtavAgi gelulx, jayisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{for a wonder} AshacxyaRkaravAgi; daMgubaDisuva riVtiyalilx: \eng{you are punctual for a wonder} elalxrU daMgAguvaMte, niVnu modalabArige hotitxge sariyAgi baMdididxVye. 
\num{3} \hyperref{kandict_n.pdf}{N}{nine(1) pagu(3)}{$^1$nine} \eng{days' wonder.} 
\hyperdef{W}{wonder(1) pagu(4)}{} 
\num{4} \eng{the seven wonders of the world} (IjipiTxna piramiDuDx \mo) pArxciVna cariterxyalilx kareyalAgiruva parxpaMcada ELu aduBxta(racane)gaLu. 
\num{5} \eng{the wonder is} idaralilx AshacxyaRveVneMdare; AshacxyaRkaravAdudeMdare. 
\hyperdef{W}{wonder(1) pagu(6)}{} 
\num{6} \eng{no} (\engit{or} \eng{small) wonder (that)} idaralelxVnU AshacxyaRvilalx; UhisabahudAda, sAvxBAvika viSaya. 
\num{7} \eng{wonders will never cease} (\sA\ AshacxyaRkaravAdarU iSaTxveV eMbaudanunx sUcisuva mAtAgi) idu nijavAgi AshacxyaRveV sari! 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{vuDf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\Eva\ yA \bava dalilx) vana; kADu; aDavi; jaMgalu; araNayx. 
\numi{2} 
\banum
\alnum{a} mara; marada -- dAru, reMbe, kAMDa. 
\alnum{b} (bAgilu, kiTaki, uravalu, \mo vugaLige baLasuva) mara; dAru; cwbiVne; swde; kaTiTxge. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (madayx tuMbida) piVpAyi \mo vu: \eng{from the wood} piVpAyiyiMda tegeda(madayx). 
\num{4} (bwlfsx ATa) = \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bowl(2)}{$^2$bowl(1)}. 
\num{5} (gAlfPx) marada taleya doNeNx.

\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\hyperdef{W}{wood pagu(1)}{} 
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{don't hallo till you are out of the wood} (\engit{or} \ame\ \eng{woods)} kaSaTxgaLanunx dATuva tanaka higagxbeVDa; kaSaTxgaLu mugidavu eMdu Barxmisi higagxbeVDa. 
\num{2} \eng{knock (on) wood} (\ame) = \hyperlink{wood pagu5}{?pagu? \((5)\)}. 
\num{3} \eng{not see the wood for the trees} vivaragaLige atiyAda gamanakoTuTx muKayx viSayavanunx kANadAgu, gamanisadiru; giDagaLanunx noVDuvalilx, eNisutAtx kADanunx mare, kANadiru. 
\num{4} \eng{out of the wood} (\engit{or} \eng{woods)} kaSaTxgaLanunx kaLedu; apAyavanunx kaDehAyudx. 
\hypertarget{wood pagu5}{} 
\numi{5} \eng{touch wood} 
\banum
\alnum{a} mara yA marada vasutxvanenxVnAdarU muTuTx; (amaMgaLavanunx nivArisali eMdu heVLuva) `biDatu' anunx(va mAtu). 
\alnum{b} (makakxLu ATadalilx sikikxbiVLuvudanunx tapipxsikoLaLxlu heVLuva) `biDatu, biDatu'. 
\eanum
\numie

\bentry
\word[word(1)]{word} 
\pron{vaDfR} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} mAtu; shabadx; pada; nuDi; solulx: \eng{is not the word for it} adakekx takakx padavalalx. 
\num{2} kaMpUyxTarf datAtxMsha, nideRVshana, \mo vugaLalilx baLasuva, mUlaBUta aBivayxkitxya GaTaka, aMsha. 
\num{3} mAtu; BASaNa: \eng{honest in word and deed} nuDiyalilx matutx naDeyalilx pArxmANika; nuDidaMte naDeyuva (niSeThxyuLaLx). 
\num{4} (\bava\ yA \Eva dalilx) heVLida mAtu; heVLike; nuDi; TiVke; ukitx; vacana; mAtukate. 
\num{5} (\bava dalilx) mAtu; hADina sAhitayx, naTana mAtugaLu, \mo vu. 
\num{6} (keVvala bAyimAtinalilx) heVLidudu; mAtu; nuDi (kAyaRrUpavAgi mADidudalalx): \eng{bold in word only} mAtinalalxSeTxV dheYyaRshAli. 
\num{7} sudidx; vAteR; samAcAra: \eng{send word} samAcAra kaLuhisu. 
\num{8} ADida mAtu; koTaTx vacana; vAgAdxna: \eng{gave us their word} avaru vAgAdxna mADidaru, mAtu koTaTxru. 
\num{9} Ajecnx; apapxNe; shAsana: \eng{his word is law} avana mAteV shAsana. 
\num{10} saMkeVta pada: \eng{gave the word to begin} pArxraMBisalu saMkeVta(pada) koTaTx. 
\num{11} sUkitx; dheyxVya(pada). 
\num{12} (\bava dalilx) koVpada mAtu; jagaLa: \eng{have words with} koVpadiMda -- nuDi, kUgADu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{at a word} heVLida yA keVLida kUDaleV. 
\num{2} \eng{a word to the wise} viveVkige oMdu mAtu sAku. 
\num{3} \eng{be as good as word} (\engit{or} \eng{better than) one's word} nuDidaMte naDe; ADidaMte (yA ADidudakikxMta migilAgi) naDeduko. 
\num{4} \eng{break one's word} mAtige tapupx. 
\num{5} \hyperref{kandict_e.pdf}{E}{eat nuga(7)}{eat} \eng{one's words.} 
\num{6} \eng{give} (\engit{or} \eng{pledge) person word} mAtu, BASe -- koDu; vAgAdxna mADu. 
\num{7} \eng{(hard, high, etc.) words} koVpada, biru -- mAtugaLu. 
\num{8} \eng{have a word (with)} saMkeSxVpavAgi mAtukate naDesu, vicAra vinimaya mADiko. 
\num{9} \eng{have a word to say} heVLalu yA keVLalu yoVgayxvAdaMtha viSayavanunx tiLidiru. 
\num{10} \eng{have no words for} mAtilalxdaMtAgu; heVLalu mAtilalxvAgu 
\num{11} \eng{his word is (as good as) his bond} avana mAteV oMdu patarx(daSuTx Kacita, satayx). 
\num{12} \eng{I give you my word for it} adu hAgeyeV, nija, eMdu Baravase koDutetxVne, parxmANa mADutetxVne. 
\num{13} \eng{in a} (\engit{or} \eng{one) word} oMdu mAtinalilx; saMkeSxVpavAgi. 
\num{14} \eng{in other words} athARtf; aMdare; beVre mAtugaLalilx heVLuvudAdare. 
\num{15} \eng{in so many words} sapxSaTxvAgi; nisasxMdigadhxvAgi; yAva saMdeVhavU ilalxdaMte. 
\hyperdef{W}{word(1) pagu(16)}{} 
\num{16} \eng{keep one's word} mAtu uLisiko; vAgAdxna pAlisu. 
\num{17} \eng{my} (\engit{or} \eng{upon my) word} (AshacxyaR yA BayasUcaka avayxyavAgi) ayoyxV deVvareV! (itAyxdi). 
\num{18} \eng{not a word of it} (kathe, vaqtAtxMta, \mo vugaLa \vi) adara bagegx -- oMdu mAtilalx, solilxlalx, sadidxlalx. 
\num{19} \eng{not have a word to throw at a dog} nAyiyanunx mAtanADisalU bAyi biDadaSuTx bigitukoMDidAdxne; mAtanADidare mututx suridu hoVgutatxdeVnoV eMdu tuTi bicacxdidAdxne. 
\num{20} \eng{not the word for it} (hAgeMdare) adakekx sariyAda, samapaRkavAda -- padavalalx; adanunx sariyAgi vivarisidaMtAgalilalx. 
\num{21} \eng{of few words} mitaBASiyAda; hecucx mAtilalxda. 
\num{22} \eng{of many words} vAcALiyAda; vipariVta mAtanADuva. 
\num{23} \eng{of one's words} mAtige tapapxda; ADida mAtinaMte naDeyuva; (avana) mAtanunx -- necacxbahudAda, naMbabahudAda: \eng{a man of his word} mAtige tapapxda vayxkitx. 
\num{24} \eng{say a few words} eraDu mAtanADu; cikakx BASaNamADu. 
\num{25} \eng{say the word} apapxNe (Ajecnx) koDu. 
\num{26} \eng{suit the action to the word} ADidaMte naDe; (bedarike, ecacxrike, \mo vanunx) nidARkiSxNayxvAgi kAyaRrUpakekx taMdubiDu. 
\hyperdef{W}{word(1) pagu(27)}{} 
\num{27} \eng{take a person at his} (\engit{or} \eng{her) word} obabx vayxkitxya mAtugaLanunx akaSxrashaH garxhisu, athaRmADiko. 
\num{28} \eng{take a person's word for it} avanu heVLidadxnunx (vicAra, shoVdhane mADade) satayxveMdu opipxko, naMbau. 
\numi{29} \eng{the Word (of God)} 
\banum
\alnum{a} beYbalulx; beYbalulx yA adara oMdu BAga. 
\alnum{b} (deVvamAnavara madhayxvatiR athavA parxtayxkaSx deVvasavxrUpaneMdu kerxYsatxru naMbauva) yeVsukirxsatx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{30} \eng{too funny etc. for words} heVLalAradaSuTx vicitarx, hAsAyxsapxda, itAyxdi. 
\num{31} \eng{upon} (\engit{or} \eng{on) my word} nananx ANegU, satayxvAgi heVLutetxVne... itAyxdi. 
\num{32} \eng{word for word} padashaH; shabadxkekx parxtiyAgi shabadx iTuTx: \eng{translate word for word} padashaH BASAMtarisu. 
\hyperdef{W}{word(1) pagu(33)}{} 
\num{33} \eng{word of honour} gwravada ANe; tananx gwravada meVle ANe iTuTx mADida vAgAdxna, koTaTx mAtu. 
\hyperdef{W}{word(1) pagu(34)}{} 
\num{34} \eng{word of mouth} keVvala bAyimAtu, heVLike. 
\num{35} \eng{words} \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{fail(2) nuga}{$^2$fail} \eng{me.} 
\num{36} \eng{words of command} (ATa, seYnika kavAyatu, \mo vugaLalilx) Ajecnxya mAtu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[word(2)]{word} 
\pron{vaDfR} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng

\bentry
\word{wordage}

\bentry
\word[work(1)]{work} 
\pron{vakfR} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} kelasa; kirxye; geYme; mATa; kAyaR; kamaR; oMdu udedxVshasAdhanegAgi mAnasika yA deYhika shakitxya parxyoVga. 
\num{2} (keYgoLaLxbeVkAda) kAyaR; kelasa; udayxma. 
\num{3} (keYgoMDa kelasakekx beVkAda) sAdhanasAmagirx; kAyoRVpakaraNagaLu; sAdhanasalakaraNegaLu. 
\num{4} nidiRSATxvadhiya kelasa: \eng{the work of a moment} kaSxNada kelasa. 
\num{5} kaqti; kelasadiMda mADidudx yA sAdhisidudx; sAdhane. 
\num{6} (vayxkitxya) udoyxVga; nwkari; jiVvanoVpAya; \kanmu\ AdAya gaLisalu avalaMbisida kelasa: \eng{looked for work} kelasakAkxgi, udoyxVgakAkxgi huDukida. \eng{is out of work} kelasavilalxde idAdxne; nirudoyxVgiyAgidAdxne. 
\numi{7} 
\banum
\alnum{a} sAhitayxda yA saMgiVtada kaqti, garxMtha: \eng{a learned work} pAMDitayxda kaqti. 
\alnum{b} (\bava dalilx) leVKaka, saMgiVtaracanekAra, \mo vara oTuTx kaqtigaLu, samagarxgarxMthagaLu: \eng{the works of Plato} pelxVToVna (samagarx)kaqtigaLu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} nidiRSaTx bageya kAyaRgaLu yA anuBavagaLu: \eng{good work} oLeLxya kelasa, satAkxyaR. \eng{thirsty work} bAyArisuva kelasa; bAyArike uMTumADuva kelasa. 
\num{9} (\bava dalilx) yaMtarxda -- kAyARMgagaLu, kAyaRBAgagaLu. 
\num{10} (\bava dalilx) (\AmA) sakala; savaR; siguva yA beVkAgiruva elalxvU. 
\num{11} (\bava dalilx) kaTaTxDa kelasa yA marAmatutx; kAmagAri (kelasa): \eng{road works} rasetx kelasa yA rasetx kAmagAri. 
\num{12} (\bava dalilx, \sA\ \Eva vAgi \parx) kAyARlaya; kAKARne; tayArikeya jAga: \eng{iron works} kabibxNada kAKARne. \eng{the works are closed next week} kAKARne muMdinavAra mucicxrutatxde. 
\num{13} (\sA\ \bava dalilx) (\deVva) puNayxkAyaR; satakxmaR. 
\num{14} (\sA\ \bava dalilx yA \saMpa dalilx) dugaR; koVTe; rakaSxNAtamxka kaTaTxDa: \eng{the works are impregnable} koVTekotatxlagaLu aBeVdayxvAgive. \eng{earthworks} maNiNxna koVTe. 
\num{15} (\pArxparx) = \hyperref{kandict_n.pdf}{N}{needlework}{needlework}. 
\num{16} (\Bwvi) kirxye; kirxyAshakitx; parxtiroVdhavanunx niBAyisuvudaralilxna yA aNuvayxtAyxsa mADuvudaralilxna shakitxparxyoVga: \eng{convert heat into work} uSaNxvanunx kirxyAshakitxyAgi parivatiRsu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{a good day's work} dinapUtiRya, dinaBatiRya -- kelasa. 
\num{2} \eng{all work and no play} (kirxVDe, manaraMjane, \mo vugaLu oMdU ilalxda) bariV duDita; EkatAnada kelasa. 
\hyperdef{W}{work(1)pagu(3)}{} 
\num{3} \eng{at work} kelasadalilx toDagi; kAyaRniratavAgi. 
\num{4} \eng{a work of art} kalAkaqti; oLeLxya vaNaRcitarx, padayx, kaTaTxDa, \mo vu. 
\num{5} \eng{beaten works} baDidu tayArisida sAmAnu. 
\num{6} \eng{embossed works} ubaubx ketatxne sAmAnu. 
\numi{7} \eng{give a person the works } (\AmA) 
\banum
\alnum{a} vayxkitxge elalxvanUnx koDu yA tiLisu. 
\alnum{b} vayxkitxyanunx goVLu hoyudxko, citarxhiMse mADu. 
\alnum{c} vayxkitxyanunx -- kolulx, sAyisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} \eng{have one's work cut out} kaThiNavAda yA diVGaRkAlada kelasa hoMdiru. 
\num{9} \eng{internal work} (oMdu vasutxvina aNugaLa meVle parxyoVgavAguva) AMtarika kirxyAshakitx. 
\num{10} \eng{many hands make light work} janavidadxSUTx kelasa hagura (Agutatxde). 
\num{11} \eng{public works} sakARrada paravAgi naDasuva kaTaTxDada yA marAmatutx kAmagAri kelasa. 
\num{12} \eng{works council} (\kanmu\ \birx) kamaRcAri maMDali; mAliVkaroDane mAtukate naDasuva kAmiRkara muKaMDaru. 
\num{13} \eng{works of} \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{supererogation pagu}{supererogation}.

\bentry
\word[work(2)]{work} 
\pron{vakfR} 
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{worked.}).}


\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (yaMtarx \mo vanunx) naDasu; kelasa mADisu; cAlU mADu: \eng{it is worked by electricity} viduyxtitxniMda (yaMtarx) naDeyutatxde. 
\num{2} kelasa mADisu; duDisu; kAyARcaraNeyalilxruvaMte, naDeyutitxruvaMte mADu: \eng{this mine is no longer worked} I gaNi kelasa mADutitxlalx. 
\num{3} naDasu; nivaRhisu; niyaMtirxsu: \eng{cannot work the machine} yaMtarxvanunx naDesalAguvudilalx. 
\num{4} (BUmiyanunx) uLu; kaqSimADu; sAguvaLi mADu. 
\num{5} uMTumADu; sAdhisu; pariNAmavAgi taru: \eng{worked miracles} pavADagaLanunx mADida. \eng{works wonders} aduBxtavAgi kelasa mADutatxde. 
\num{6} beVkAda hadakekx, rUpakekx, mATakekx -- taru, nAdu, baDi: \eng{work dough} hiTaTxnunx nAdu. \eng{work butter thoroughly} beNeNxyanunx oLeLxya hadakekx kaDe. 
\num{7} kasUti hAku; kasUti kelasa mADu: \eng{she is working a shawl} avaLu shAlige kasUti hAkutitxdAdxLe. 
\num{8} (nidiRSaTx riVtiyalilx, kaSaTxdiMda yA karxmeVNa) nugigxsu; hogisu; dArimADi koMDu hoVguvaMte mADu: \eng{worked our way through the crowd} guMpina naDuve nugigx dArimADikoMDu sAgidevu, hoVdevu. \eng{worked the peg into the hole} beNeyanunx tUtinoLakekx hogisidevu. 
\num{9} kaqtakavAgi uderxVkisu, keraLisu: \eng{worked themselves into a rage} koVpa -- keraLisikoMDaru, barisikoMDaru. 
\num{10} (gaNitada parxshenxyanunx) biDisu; bageharisu; utatxra kaMDuhiDi. 
\numi{11} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (haNakekx badalAgi) duDidu, duDimeya mUlaka -- koMDuko, saMpAdisu: \eng{work} \eng{one's passage} tananx parxyANada KacaRnunx kelasada mUlaka salilxsida. 
\alnum{b} vecacxda haNavanunx duDimeya mUlaka -- gaLisu, paDeduko: \eng{work one's way through the university} vishavxvidAyxnilayada Odina haNavanunx duDidu gaLisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} kelasa, kAyaR -- mADu; sharxmisu; duDi; shAriVraka yA mAnasika kelasadalilx niratanAgu. 
\num{2} (yAvudeV) udoyxVgadalilx, kelasadalilx neVmaka paDediru: \eng{works in industry} keYgArikoVdayxmadalilx udoyxVga mADutAtxne. \eng{work as a secretary} kAyaRdashiRyAgi kelasa mADu. 
\num{3} sharxmisu; parxyatanxmADu; kAyARcaraNe, caLavaLi naDesu: \eng{works for peace} shAMtigAgi sharxmisutAtxne. 
\num{4} (vishiSaTx padAthaRdalilx) kelasa mADu; kushalakamiRyAgiru: \eng{works in brass} hitAtxLe kelasa mADutAtxne. 
\num{5} (\kanmu\ pariNAmakAriyAgi) kelasa -- mADu, naDesu: \eng{how does the machine work ?} yaMtarx heVge kelasa mADutatxde? \eng{your idea does not work} ninanx aBipArxya kAyaRkAriyAgilalx. 
\num{6} (yaMtarxBAgada \vi) ODu; ADu; naDe; tirugu; kelasa mADu: \eng{wheel works freely} cakarx sarAgavAgi tirugutatxde. 
\num{7} kaSaTxdiMda yA nidhAnavAgi -- calisu, sAgu, muMduvare: \eng{work upstream} nadiya meVlumuKavAgi hoVgu. 
\num{8} (satata calaneyiMda) karxmeVNa saDila, aLaLxka, \mo vu Agu 
\num{9} kuSxbadhxvAgu (\rUpa\ saha): \eng{face worked violently} muKa tiVvarxvAgi parxkuSxbadhxvAyitu. 
\num{10} (nwkeya \vi) gALige virudadhxvAgi, edurAgi -- sAgu, hoVgu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{set to work} 
\banum
\alnum{a} kelasakekx keYhacucx, toDagu; kelasa pArxraMBisu. 
\alnum{b} kelasakekx hacucx, toDagisu; kelasa pArxraMBa mADuvaMte mADu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{work an idea to death} (yAvudAdarU vicAra \mo vanunx) atiyAgi, savakalAguvaMte baLasu. 
\num{3} \eng{work away} (\engit{or} \eng{on)} (biDade) kelasa -- mADutitxru, muMduvaresu. 
\num{4} \eng{work in} (nidashaRna, saMgati, \mo vanunx) heVgoV oLakekx tUrisu; sathxLa mADi, avakAsha kalipxsi, oLakekx -- heNe, neVyi, seVrisu. 
\num{5} \eng{work one's fingers to the} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bone(1) nuga(13)}{$^1$bone}. 
\num{6} \eng{work one's} \hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{passage(1) pagu(2)}{$^1$passage}. 
\num{7} \eng{work it} (\AmA) sAdhisu; uMTumADu; udidxSaTx PalitAMsha paDe. 
\numi{8} \eng{work off} 
\banum
\alnum{a} kelasa mADi -- nivArisiko, pariharisiko, tiVrisiko, kaLeduko, kaDame mADiko: \eng{works his bad temper on his servants} tananx koVpavanunx ALugaLa meVle tiVrisikoLuLxtAtxne, ALugaLa meVle koVpa toVrisi nivArisikoLuLxtAtxne. \eng{worked off his debt} duDidu tananx sAla tiVrisikoMDa. \eng{work off excess of weight} atiyAda tUkavanunx kaLeduko, kaDame mADiko. 
\alnum{b} (vasutxgaLige girAki \mo varanunx hoMdisi) mArihAku; vileVvAri mADu: \eng{worked off} \eng{3000} \eng{copies} mUrusAvira parxtigaLanunx mArihAkida. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{9} \eng{work one's will} (\AmA) tananx udedxVsha sAdhisiko, IDeVrisiko. 
\numi{10} \eng{work out} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (gaNitada) lekakxmADu; lekakxkekx utatxra kaMDuhiDi; lekakxda parxshenx biDisu. 
\alnum{b} motatx kaMDuhiDi; eNisu. 
\alnum{c} motatx Agu: \eng{the total works out at Rs. 2000} lekAkxcAradalilx, motatxdalilx adu \eng{2000} rUpAyigaLAgutatxde. 
\alnum{d} (lekakxda \vi) mADalAgu; mADabaru; nidiRSaTx PalitAMsha niVDu: \eng{this sum will not work out} I lekakxvanunx mADalAguvudilalx. 
\alnum{e} vishiSaTx PalitAMsha hoMdiru: \eng{the plan worked out well} yoVjane saPalavAyitu. 
\alnum{f} vivaragaLanunx aNigoLisu; kUlaMkaSavAgi yoVjisu: \eng{has worked out a scheme} yoVjaneyoMdanunx tayArisidAdxne. 
\alnum{g} parxyatanxpaTuTx, kaSaTxpaTuTx -- sAdhisu, gaLisu, paDe: \eng{worked out one's salavation} parxyatanx mADi tananx mukitx sAdhisikoMDa. 
\alnum{h} kelasadiMda -- baridAgu, KAliyAgu: \eng{the mine is worked out} toVDitoVDi gaNi KAliyAgide. 
\alnum{i} kelasadiMda -- susAtxgu, baLalu, AyAsa hoMdu: \eng{the person is worked out} avanu duDidu susAtxgidAdxne. 
\alnum{j} deYhika vAyxyAmadalilx toDagu 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{11} \eng{work over} 
\banum
\alnum{a} pUtiR, AdayxMtavAgi -- pariVkiSxsu, taniKe mADu. 
\alnum{b} (\AmA) keYmADu; baDi; cacucx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{12} \eng{work to rule} (\kanmu\ keYgArikA keVSxtarxdalilx utapxnanx matutx dakaSxte tagigxsalu parxtiBaTaneya vidhAnavAgi) niyamaparxkAradaSeTxV, niyama parxkAradaSuTx mAtarxveV -- kelasa mADu. 
\numi{13} \eng{work up} 
\banum
\alnum{a} karxmeVNa, nidhAnavAgi -- samathaR sithxtige taru. 
\alnum{b} karxmeVNa, nidhAnavAgi paramAvadhiya maTaTxkekx, sithxtige -- baru, sAgu, sari; karxmeVNa -- shiKara muTuTx, parAkASeThx talupu. 
\alnum{c} karxmeVNa visAtxravAgi -- nirUpisu, visatxrisu. 
\alnum{d} karxmeVNa (vayxkitx, BAva, BAvanegaLanunx) ebibxsu; uderxVkagoLisu. 
\alnum{e} (parikara padAthaRgaLanunx) cenAnxgi berasu; samimxsharxmADu; samimxLanagoLisu. 
\alnum{f} (viSayavanunx) vAyxsaMgamADu; Odu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{14} \eng{work with a person} obabxna jote kelasa mADu, sahoVdoyxVgiyAgiru. 
\num{15} \eng{yeast began to work up} maMDa, kiNavx -- hudugeVLatoDagitu. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[world(1)]{world} 
\pron{valfRDx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
% 
\bnum
\num{1} loVka; parxpaMca; jagatutx. 
\num{2} lwkikAsakitxgaLu; pArxpaMcika vAyxpAragaLu, vayxvahAragaLu; aihika parxloVBanegaLu. 
\numi{3} 
\banum
\alnum{a} vishavx; saqSiTx; samasatx; savaRsavx: \eng{the best of all possible worlds} saqSiTxyalelxlAlx atuyxtatxma saqSiTx. 
\alnum{b} samasatxjana; loVka; mAnavasamaSiTx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} (tananxnunx biTuTx) horagaNa loVka; bAhayx parxpaMca: \eng{dead to the world} horaparxpaMcakekx satatx, maqtapArxyanAda. 
\num{5} loVkada -- savaRsavxvU, samasatxvU: \eng{she is all the world to me} nananx savaRsavxvU avaLeV. 
\num{6} BUmi; BUloVka; BUmaMDala yA adaraMthadeV garxhakAya: \eng{go round the world} parxpaMcavanunx sututx. 
\num{7} parxpaMcada deVshagaLu matutx avugaLa nivAsigaLu. 
\num{8} mAnava vAyxpAra; loVkavayxvahAra; loVkada -- riVtiniVti matutx sithxtigatigaLu; aihika jiVvana; saMsAra; lwkika : \eng{so wags the world} hiVge I loVka naDeyutAtx baMdide. 
\num{9} (sAmAnayx dajeRya, gwravasathx yA navanAjUkina) jana; samAja; sAmAjika -- padadhxti, aBipArxya. 
\num{10} loVka; vishavx; parxpaMca; vishiSaTx vagaRda, valayada, keSxVtarxda jana matutx avarige saMbaMdhisida sakalavU: \eng{the literary world} \engit{or} \eng{the world of letters} sAhitigaLa loVka; sAhitayx parxpaMca. \eng{the medieval world} madhayxyugada samAja. \eng{the world of sport} kirxVDA parxpaMca. 
\num{11} BAri motatx; apAra saMKeyx; apAra visAtxra: \eng{a world of meaning} barxhAmxMDa athaR. \eng{a world of difference} BAri vayxtAyxsa. 
\num{12} mAnava jagatutx; jiVvanada kAla, sithxti yA daqshayx. 
\num{13} mataRyxjiVvana; mataRyxloVka. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{a world} (\engit{or} \eng{worlds) too wide} bahumaTiTxge; bahaLaSuTx. 
\numi{2} \eng{all the world and his wife.} 
\banum
\alnum{a} navanAjUkanunx parxdashiRsuva sakalarU. 
\alnum{b} nAnA bageya janagaLiruva doDaDx guMpu, samUha, saBe. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{all's right with the world} parxpaMcadalilx, badukinalilx elalxvU sariyAgide (EnU korateyilalx, keTaTxdudx yAvudU ilalx eMba AshAvAdada sUtorxVkitx). 
\num{4} \eng{all the world knows} loVkakekxlAlx tiLidide; elalxrigU gotutx; jagajAjxhiVrAgide. 
\num{5} \eng{(all) the world over} vishavxdalelxlAlx; parxpaMcada elAlx kaDe. 
\numi{6} \eng{bring into the world} 
\banum
\alnum{a} huTiTxniMdaleV paDe; Ajanamx pArxpatxvAgiru; janamxtaH, huTuTxtAtx -- taru. 
\alnum{b} (herigeya \vi) haDeyalu, heralu neravAgu; herige mADisu. 
\alnum{c} (maguvanunx) haDe; heru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{7} \eng{carry the world before one} kiSxparxvAgi pUNaRjaya sAdhisu; beVga pUtiR gelulx; shiVGarxvAgi pUNaRyashasusx gaLisu. 
\num{8} \eng{come into the world} huTuTx; janamxtALu. 
\num{9} \eng{for all the world (like} \engit{or} \eng{as if)} karAruvAkAkxgi; KacitavAgi; niKaravAgi; tadavxtAtxgi: \eng{looked for all the world as if they were real} avu nijavAgiruvaMteyeV, satayxsaMgatiyeMbaMteyeV kaMDavu. 
\numi{10} \eng{get the best of both worlds} 
\banum
\alnum{a} ihaparagaLeraDanUnx sAdhisu; lwkika matutx AdhAyxtimxka eraDara lABavanUnx, parxyoVjanavanUnx gaLisu, paDeduko. 
\alnum{b} parasapxra virudadhxvAgi kANuva eraDU gurigaLanunx, dheyxVyagaLanunx sAdhisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{11} \eng{give to the world} parxkaTisu; bahiraMgagoLisu.

\bentry 
\word[worry(1)]{worry} 
\pron{vari}
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (nAyiya \vi) (ili, kuri, matotxMdu nAyi, \mo vanunx) matetxmatetx kacucx; kacicxkoMDu jagugx, eLedADu. 
\num{2} meVliMda meVle AkarxmaNa, halelx -- naDesu. 
\num{3} kADu; goVLADisu; piVDisu; kirukuLa, kATa, manaHkelxVsha -- koDu; goVLu hoyudxko. 
\num{4} (\BUkaq dalilx) bahaLa peVcATadalilxru; caDapaDisutitxru; odAdxDutitxru: \eng{he is worried about his son} tananx magana bagegx avanu peVcATadalilxdAdxne. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
peVcADu; caDapaDisu; kelxVsha, taLamaLa, kirikiri, AtaMka -- paDu; manasisxge vayxthehacicxko. 
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{I should worry} (\AmA) adariMda nanageVnU ciMteyilalx; adanunx nAnu hacicx koLuLxvudilalx. 
\num{2} \eng{be much} (\engit{or} \eng{very) worried} tuMbA peVcATadalilxru. 
\num{3} \eng{not to worry} (\AmA) sumamxne yoVcane mADabeVDa; adara bagegx ciMtisuva agatayxvilalx. 
\num{4} \eng{wears a worried look} peVcATadalilxruvaMte kANutAtxne. 
\num{5} \eng{worry oneself} kelxVshapaDu; anAvashayxkavAgi toMdare hacicxko, manasisxge hacicxko.

\bentry
\word{would} 
\pron{vuDf, vaDf sahAyaka} 
\gl{\kirx}
\bmng
(\parxpu\ \Eva\ \eng{would}) (\eng{will} \kirx da \BU). (\kanmu\ keLagina saMdaBaRgaLalilx baLake): 
\bnum
\numi{1} divxtiVya matutx parxthama puruSagaLalilx, matutx kelavomemx utatxma puruSadalUlx saha = \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{should(1)}{should(1)}: 
\banum
\alnum{a} paroVkaSx varadiyalilx: \eng{he said he would be home by evening} sAyaMkAlada hotitxge manege baruveneMdu avanu heVLida. 
\alnum{b} saMBAvanAsUcaka kirxyeyanunx sUcisalu: \eng{they would have been killed if they had gone} oMdu veVLe avaru hoVgididxdadxre avaru koleyAgutitxdadxru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} rUDhiya yA dinaMparxtiya kelasavanunx sUcisalu: \eng{would wait for her every evening} parxtidina saMje avaLigAgi kAyutitxdadx. 
\num{3} parxshenx yA namarx beVDikeyanunx sUcisalu: \eng{would they like it?} adanunx avaru iSaTxpaDuvareV? \eng{would you come in, please?} dayaviTuTx, oLage baruvirA? 
\num{4} saMBavaniVyateyanunx sUcisalu: \eng{I guess she would be over fifty by now} sadayxkekx Ake aivatatxnunx dATidAdxLeMdu nananx Uhe. 
\num{5} (sAhitayxka) iSaTxvanunx sUcisalu: \eng{would that you were here} niVvu ililx iruvaMtAdare nanage cenAnxgirutitxtutx. 
\num{6} opipxgeyanunx sUcisalu: \eng{they would not help} avaru sahAya mADuvudilalx, mADalopupxvudilalx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\gl{\kirx}

 \eng{wrapping}).

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (kAgada \mo vugaLiMda) sututx; sutitxDu; hodisu; mucucx; AcACxdisu: \eng{wrap it in paper} kAgadadalilx sututx. 
\num{2} (\rUpa) (hima, atiyAda mAtu, rahasayx, \mo vugaLiMda) Avarisu; AcACxdisu; mucucx; mucicxru: \eng{affair is wrapped in mystery} saMgati rahasayxdalilx mucicxkoMDide, AcACxditavAgide. 
\num{3} hodisu; mucucx; cenAnxgi sututx: \eng{wrapped her shawl closer about her} avaLu tananx shAlanunx cenAnxgi hodudxkoMDaLu. 
\num{4} (\ashi) (vAhanada \vi) niMtiruva vasutxvige -- gududx, DikikxhoDe, saMGaTiTxsu.

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{wrap over} (uDupina \vi) dharisidAga (oMdara meVloMdu hodisidaMte) mucicx hoVgu 
\numi{2} \eng{wrap up} 
\banum
\alnum{a} hodudxko; (meY \mo vanunx) mucicxko: \eng{mind you, wrap up well if you go out} joVke, niVnu horage hoVdare, becacxge hodeduko. 
\alnum{b} (\ashi, AjAcnxthaRka) tepapxgiru; sumamxniru. 
\alnum{c} mugisibiDu; itayxthaR mADu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{wrap up meaning} athaR mucicxbiDu; jaTilavAgisu: \eng{he wraps up his meaning in tortuous sentences} avanu tananx mAtina athaRvanunx aMkuDoMkAgi tirucida vAkayxgaLalilx mucicxDutAtxne. 
\num{4} \eng{wrapped up} maganxvAgiru; talilxVnavAgiru; muLugiru: \eng{the mother is wrapped up in her child} tAyi maguvina keSxVmapoVSaNegaLalilx maganxLAgidAdxLe.

\gl{\kirx}
\expl{}
\bmng

\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng

\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{write} 
\pron{reYTf} 
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ \eng{wrote} \ucAcx\ roVTf, \pArxparx\ \eng{writ}}
\ucAcx\ riTf; \BUkaq\  \eng{written} \ucAcx\ riTanf). 

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} bare; leVKisu; saMkeVta, akaSxra yA padagaLanunx bare. 
\num{2} (kAgada, hALe, cekukx, \mo vugaLanunx) bare; barehadiMda tuMbau: \eng{has written three sheets} mUru puTa baredidAdxne. 
\num{3} gaNakayaMtarxda yA kaMpUyxTarina koVshakekx (mAhitiyanunx) -- tuMbau, seVrisu, dAKale mADu. 
\num{4} (\kaparx dalilx yA \BUkaq dalilx) guNa, sithxti, \mo vanunx -- sUcisu, mudirxsu, aMkisu: \eng{has honesty written on his face} pArxmANikate avana muKada meVle aMkitavAgide (avanu pArxmANika eMbaudanunx avana muKaveV sUcisutatxde). 
\num{5} (garxMtha, leVKana, kavana, \mo vanunx) bare; racisu; parxkaTanegAgi liKitarUpa koDu: \eng{has written ten novels} hatutx kAdaMbarigaLanunx baredidAdxne. 
\num{6} (\ame\ yA \AmA) kAgada, patarx -- bare; kAgada baredu (vayxkitxge) kaLuhisu: \eng{wrote him last week} avanige kaLeda vAra (kAgada) barede. 
\num{7} kAgadada mUlaka (sudidx, samAcAra, \mo vanunx) tiLisu: \eng{write me all the news} elAlx sudidxyanUnx bare(du tiLisu). 
\num{8} liKita yA mudirxta patarxdalilx -- nirUpisu, tiLisu: \eng{it is written that} hiVgeMdu baredide, liKitavAgide. 
\num{9} dAKalAgisu; dAKalAguvaMte mADu; dAKale mADisu. 
\num{10} vimApatarxkekx opipxge sahi, ruju hAku. 
\num{11} (\pArxparx) bare; barehadalilx vaNiRsu, vivarisu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} bare; leVKisu: \eng{does not read or write} Odalu yA bareyalu bAradu. 
\num{2} (leVKana \mo vugaLanunx) bareyuvudaralilx toDagiru; bareyuva vaqtitx hiDidiru: \eng{writes for the local newspaper} sathxLiVya patirxkege bareyutAtxne. 
\num{3} kAgada, patarx baredu (vayxkitxge) kaLuhisu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{nothing to write} \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{home(3) nuga(5)}{$^3$home} \eng{about.} 
\numi{2} \eng{write down} 
\banum
\alnum{a} barediDu; dAKale mADu; barehadalilx dAKalisu. 
\alnum{b} (Odu, bareha, aMtasutx, \mo vugaLalilx keLa aMtasitxnavarigAgiyoV eMbaMte) tiLiyAgi, saraLiVkarisi bare; tagigxsi bare. 
\alnum{c} jaredu, haLidu yA lAGavavAgi bare. 
\alnum{d} (baMDavALa patarx, sarakugaLu, \mo vugaLa) muKabele, namUdubele -- tagigxsu, kaDamemADu. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{3} \eng{write in} 
\banum
\alnum{a} saMsethxyoMdakekx (\kanmu\ AkAshavANi parxsAra nilayakekx salahe, sUcane, parxshenx, \mo vanunx) bare; baredu, liKitarUpadalilx tiLisu. 
\alnum{b} (\ame) matacunAvaNeyalilx aBayxthiRgaLa paTiTxge (hecicxna yA biTuTxhoVgiruva) hesarugaLanunx seVrisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{write into} (ucita badalAvaNegaLoMdige) (hosa viSaya yA parxsaMgavanunx) seVrisu. 
\num{5} \eng{write large} dapapxnAgi, doDaDxdAgi, edudxkANuvaMte -- bare. 
\numi{6} \eng{write off.} 
\banum
\alnum{a} kAgada baredu ravAne mADu, kaLuhisu. 
\alnum{b} (vasUlAgada sAla, kaLeduhoVda sAmAnu, \mo vugaLa) dAKaleyanunx - aLisihAku, hoDeduhAku; vajA mADu; (baMDavALa, Asitx, sAmAnu, \mo vugaLa) naSaTxvanunx yA matetx paDeyalAgadiruvikeyanunx opipxko, dAKale mADu. 
\alnum{c} (vAhana \mo vanunx) ripeVri mADalAgadaSuTx nAshagoLisu, hALumADu. 
\alnum{d} saliVsAgi bare; liVlAjAlavAgi racisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{7} \eng{write out} 
\banum
\alnum{a} pUtiRyAgi yA pUNaRrUpadalilx bare; AdayxMtavAgi namUdisu, nirUpisu. 
\alnum{b} baredu susAtxgu: \eng{have written myself out} baredubaredu susAtxgidedxVne, bareyuvudakekx beVreVnU viSayavilalxdavanAgidedxVne. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} \eng{write out of} bareda kaqtiyiMda (pAtarx, GaTane, \mo vanunx) kitutx hAku; aLisi hAku. 
\num{9} \eng{writes a good hand} suMdaravAgi bareyutAtxne; avana keYbaraha, akaSxragaLu mudAdxgive. 
\numi{10} \eng{write up} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (GaTane \mo vugaLa bagegx) pUNaRvAgi bare; pUtiRvivaragaLanunx nirUpisu, koDu. 
\alnum{b} hogaLi, koMDADi, parxshaMsisi -- bare. 
\alnum{c} (dinacari pusatxka \mo vugaLalilx) dAKalegaLanunx sadayxdavarege barediDu, tahalfvarege taru. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[wrong(1)]{wrong} 
\pron{rAMgf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} tapApxda; keTuTxhoVda; vayxtayxsatxvAda; karxmatapipxda; avayxvasethxya; susithxtiyalilxlalxda: \eng{something is wrong with him} avanalilx EnoV vayxtAyxsavAgide. \eng{something is wrong with my heart} nananx haqdaya susithxtiyalilxlalx. \eng{my watch has gone wrong} nananx gaDiyAra keTuTxhoVgide. 
\num{2} tapApxda; sariyalalxda; nijasithxtigiMta yA vAsatxva saMgatigiMta BinanxvAda: \eng{gave a wrong answer} tapu px utatxra koTaTx. 
\num{3} tapApxda; beVkilalxda; beVDavAda; anapeVkiSxtavAda; opipxgeyAgada : \eng{the wrong road} tapu px rasetx; beVkirada rasetx. \eng{a wrong decision} tapu px tiVmARna; yukitxyukatxvAgirada, opipxgeyAgada -- tiVmARna. 
\num{4} tapApxda; ucitavalalxda; yukatxvalalxda; takukxdalalxda: \eng{he always says the wrong thing} avanu yAvAgalU ayukatxvAdudanenxV heVLutAtxne. 
\num{5} anAyxyada; adhamaRda; duSaTx; pApada; keTaTxdAda; kAnUnige yA niVtige virudadhxvAda: \eng{it is wrong to steal} kadiyuvudu keTaTxdudx. \eng{took the wrong way} keTaTxdAri, anAyxyada mAgaR hiDida. \eng{a wrong deed} pApakaqtayx; duSaTxkAyaR. 
\num{6} kAyaR, tiVmARna yA vidhAnadalilx -- sariyalalxda, sariyAgirada: \eng{you are wrong to blame him} niVnu avananunx bayuyxvudu sariyalalx, tapupx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{get} (\engit{or} \eng{hold of) the wrong end of the stick} (\rUpa) athaRmADikoLuLxvalilx pUtiR tapupxmADu, tapApxgiru; saMpUNaRvAgi tapapxthaR mADiko. 
\num{2} \eng{get on the wrong side of} (obabxna) avagarxhakekx, avakaqpege -- biVLu, pAtarxnAgu. 
\num{3} \eng{go down the wrong way} (AhAra) ananxnALakekx badalAgi shAvxsanALakekx hoVgu; tapu pxnALadoLakekx iLi. 
\numi{4} \eng{in the wrong box} 
\banum
\alnum{a} kilxSaTx parisithxtiyalilx. 
\alnum{b} parxtikUla parisithxtiyalilx. 
\alnum{c} ikakxTiTxna yA peVcina yA mujugarada parisithxtiyalilx. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{5} \eng{on the wrong side of} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxya) avakaqpege oLagAda. 
\alnum{b} (heVLida, namUdisida vayasisxgiMta) savxlapx hecAcxgiruva. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{(the) wrong way round} rUDhiya yA yukatxvAda mAgaRkekx, daqSiTxkoVnakekx -- edurina yA virudadhxvAda mAgaR yA daqSiTxkoVna. 
\num{7} \eng{what is wrong with...?} (\AmA) adaralelxVnu doVSa, tapipxde? (adakekx badaliyAgi beVre yAvudaradU agatayxvilalx eMbathaRdalilx) adeVke -- beVDa, kUDadu? 
\num{8} \eng{wrong side out} oLa(muKa) horagAgiruva. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bmng

\num{1} tirucida; vakarx; soTaTx; oMdu kaDege tirugikoMDa. 
\num{2} (muKa, nagu, \mo vugaLa \vi) (jugupesx, nirAshe yA aNakadiMda) soTATxda; vakarx; tirucida.

\enum
\emng
